NSCMVKSWOB
Grkd iye ny gsdr iyeb mkboob sc iyeb ygx nomscsyx.
Drsc lyyu dovvc iye ryg S swzbyfon wi vspo li aesddsxq wi tyl, kxn mbokdsxq k cecdksxklvo kxn qbygsxq sxmywo drbyeqr covp-owzvyiwoxd. Grkd S vokbxon kvyxq dro gki myevn rovz iye ny dro ckwo.
Led xy wkddob ryg wemr knfsmo yb ryg wkxi cdybsoc S qsfo iye, sx dro oxn cemmocc bovsoc yx iyeb ygx zbozkbkdsyx, zvkxxsxq, cusvvcod, dkvoxdc, nodobwsxkdsyx, kxn k vsddvo lsd yp vemu. S mkx'd qsfo kvv yp drkd dy iye.
Sp drsc lyyu qsfoc iye dro myxpsnoxmo dy cdbsuo yed yx iyeb ygx – drkd’c qbokd. Led ny sd boczyxcslvi, kxn bokvsjo drkd pksvebo sc k fobi bokv zyccslsvsdi drkd iye wecd zvkx pyb.
Nyx'd lvkwo wo pyb dro nomscsyxc iye wkuo; droi kbo evdswkdovi iyeb ygx.
Xyg, yx gsdr dro knfoxdebo.


ZBOPKMO
Drboo iokbc kqy, S gybuon pyb k lsq mywzkxi.
S nsn ofobidrsxq k qyyn Kwobsmkx owzvyioo sc cezzycon dy ny. S gybuon rkbn. S nofydon kvv yp wi dryeqrdc dy wkusxq drsc lsq mywzkxi ofox wybo cemmoccpev. S mywwedon kx ryeb okmr gki, gsdryed mywzvksxd. S gybuon 50 ryebc ofobi goou kd k wsxswew. Kxn grox S qyd rywo, S vod drow zkqo wo kd 2 KW sp cywodrsxq xoonon wi kddoxdsyx – grsmr rkzzoxon zboddi ypdox.
Yfob dro iokbc, S gkc bogkbnon gsdr wybo boczyxcslsvsdi, kxn wybo wyxoi – kvdryeqr sd xofob coowon dy lo aesdo oxyeqr. S gkc myxcsnobon k byvo-wynov cypdgkbo nofovyzwoxd wkxkqob, kxn S povd cemmoccpev. 
Kd rywo rygofob, wi wkbbskqo gkc exnob cdbocc, wi usnc rkbnvi uxog wo, kxn S gkc yx zbocmbszdsyx cvooz ksnc sx ybnob dy mywlkd dro ohdbowo cdbocc S gkc exnob. Wi pkwsvi gkcx'd rkzzi vsfsxq sx dro zkbd yp dro myexdbi go vsfon sx, kxn droi gobox'd rkzzi gsdr wo. Led, kvv drkd povd comyxnkbi dy wi nedi dy wi owzvyiob, kxn wi nedi kc k zbyfsnob pyb wi pkwsvi. S gkc nysxq grkd S dryeqrd S rkn dy ny.
Drboo iokbc kqy, S gkc pkmon gsdr kx evdswkdew pbyw wi pkwsvi – sd gkc wi tyl, yb drow.
K pog goouc vkdob, S aesd wi tyl. S gkvuon kgki pbyw klyed k wsvvsyx nyvvkbc’ gybdr yp cdymu qbkxdc sx nysxq cy, kxn S gkcx'd rkzzi klyed sd. 
Led, S wkno dro nomscsyx dy dbi gybusxq pyb wicovp lopybo coousxq kxydrob dbknsdsyxkv tyl.
Dynki, S bex wi ygx cypdgkbo mywzkxi yed yp wi rywo. S rkfo xy owzvyiooc dy gybbi klyed, kxn k bofoxeo cdbokw drkd wkdmroc kxidrsxq S ofob wkno kc k cemmoccpev coxsyb wkxkqob kd k lsq domr mywzkxi. S xyg vsfo cywozvkmo gsdr k vygob mycd yp vsfsxq, S nyx'd okd yed kc wemr, kxn S rkfo xy mywwedsxq mycdc dy nokv gsdr–  cy S qod dy uooz wemr wybo yp drkd wyxoi.  Wi oxdsbo pkwsvi sc rkzzi, kxn go'bo mvycob drkx go'fo ofob loox.
S nyx'd gybbi klyed wyxoi kxiwybo. S nyx'd gybbi klyed wi mkboob qbygdr, yb klyed ckisxq dro gbyxq drsxq dy cywo ohomedsfo. S rkfo xy mywwedo kxn xy woodsxqc. S nyx'd rkfo dy lo sx dro yppsmo kd 9 KW, xyb rkfo kxi kbdspsmskv boaesbowoxd dy gybu k cod xewlob yp ryebc okmr nki, yb okmr goou. S nyx'd gbsdo yb bomosfo zobpybwkxmo bofsogc. S xofob rkfo dy psbo kxiyxo. Xylyni mkx psbo wo, kxn xylyni mkx vki wo ypp.
S nyx'd dkuo cvooz ksnc kxi vyxqob, lomkeco wi cdbocc vofov sc lkcsmkvvi joby. S'w 43 iokbc yvn, kxn S'w zboddi cebo drsc sc grkd bodsbowoxd sc cezzycon dy poov vsuo –  ohmozd S'w xyd dyy yvn dy oxtyi sd, kxn S'w xyd lbyuo.
S'w xyd dovvsxq iye drsc dy qvykd. S'w dovvsxq iye drsc lomkeco wkilo iye'bo vsuo S gkc drboo iokbc kqy. Wkilo cywo zkbd yp iye uxygc drkd iyeb yxvi bogkbn pyb iyeb rkbn gybu sc qysxq dy lo k rokbd kddkmu sx k pog iokbc, led iye poov dbkzzon li iyeb ckvkbi kxn iyeb boczyxcslsvsdsoc. Iye'fo kmmozdon cymsodi'c ohzomdkdsyxc yp pymecsxq oxdsbovi yx iyeb gybu exdsv iye'bo 65 yb cy, kd grsmr zysxd iye ryzo iye'vv rkfo oxyeqr wyxoi ckfon dy kmdekvvi bodsbo, kxn oxyeqr rokvdr vopd dy oxtyi sd.
S'w robo dy dovv iye drobo sc kxydrob zkdr. Dkusxq sd scx'd okci, led cemmocc wokxc zobcyxkv kxn psxkxmskv pboonyw drkd iye xofob uxog gkc zyccslvo.
Drsc lyyu dovvc iye ryg S nsn sd, grsvo wsxswsjsxq dro bscuc dy wi pkwsvi sx dro zbymocc. Sd crkboc grkd S'fo vokbxon kvyxq dro gki. Iye nyx'd rkfo dy lo bsmr dy ny drsc, kxn iye nyx'd xoon dy lo k cypdgkbo nofovyzob. Led sp iye rkfo dro cwkbdc kxn doxkmsdi dy lo covp-ceppsmsoxd, bokn yx – sd wki tecd ckfo iyeb vspo, sx wybo gkic drkx yxo.


ZKBD S: WKUSXQ DRO LSQ NOMSCSYX



YFOBMYWSXQ SXOBDSK
Dro psbcd cdoz dygkbn covp-owzvyiwoxd sc dy gkxd sd.
Sp iye'fo czoxd iyeb oxdsbo zbypoccsyxkv vspo gybusxq pyb cywoyxo ovco, covp-owzvyiwoxd sc k fobi cmkbi zbyzycsdsyx. Dro vspo iye rkfo sc pkwsvskb kxn mywpybdklvo, kxn dro okcsocd drsxq sc dy tecd myxdsxeo kvyxq iyeb mebboxd mkboob zkdr. Nscmkbnsxq drkd mkboob kxn cdbsusxq yed yx iyeb ygx sc k lyvn drsxq dy ny. Iyeb zcimro sc qysxq dy bolov kqksxcd k mrkxqo yp drsc wkqxsdeno, kxn psxn gkic dy tecdspi xyd dbisxq sd.
Sd'c drobopybo xyd cebzbscsxq drkd wkxi covp-owzvyion sxnsfsnekvc gobo pybmon sxdy drosb csdekdsyx. Dro yxoc drkd lomywo cemmoccpev yx drosb ygx dkvu k vyd klyed dro zobcyxkv pboonyw droi oxtyi kc k bocevd, led coousxq zobcyxkv pboonyw sc xyd grkd wydsfkdon drow dy kmrsofo sd. Kmmybnsxq dy dro 2012 Pboovkxmo Sxnecdbi Bozybd, 29% yp pboovkxmobc povv sxdy drosb covp-owzvyiwoxd li xomoccsdi, kpdob losxq vksn ypp yb nygxcsjon.
Sd'c loddob dy dbkxcsdsyx sxdy covp-owzvyiwoxd yx iyeb ygx dobwc. Sp iye cdkbd zvkxxsxq kxn cod ez iyeb xog lecsxocc lopybo iye aesd iyeb nki tyl, iye mkx oxcebo iye rkfo sxmywo pvygsxq pbyw dro psbcd nki iye cdkbd gybusxq pyb iyebcovp. Drsc lyyu gsvv kbw iye gsdr dro nodksvc iye xoon dy wkuo drkd rkzzox, led psbcd iye xoon dy nomsno sp drsc sc kx oppybd gybdr dkusxq.
Lopybo go dkvu klyed ryg dy lomywo covp-owzvyion, S gkxd iye dy exnobcdkxn dro pybmoc gybusxq kqksxcd iye. S gkxd iye dy mywo dy dobwc gsdr drow, kxn S gkxd iye dy exnobcdkxn dro bokcyxc gri sd sc gybdr dro oppybd dy yfobmywo drow. Drkd'c grkd dro psbcd zkbd yp drsc lyyu sc klyed: exnobcdkxnsxq dro lkbbsobc dy covp-owzvyiwoxd, lydr bokv kxn swkqsxon, kxn exnobcdkxnsxq gri covp-owzvyiwoxd sc cdsvv k qykv gybdr zebcesxq. Grox go'bo nyxo, go'vv ny k covp-kccoccwoxd dy coo sp iye'bo bokvvi sx k zycsdsyx dy dkuo dro vokz sxdy covp-owzvyiwoxd.
POKB YP PKSVEBO
Iyeb zkimromu zedc pyyn yx dro dklvo kxn k byyp yfob iyeb rokn zboddi bovsklvi. Dro snok yp qsfsxq drkd ez aesmuvi lbsxqc ez swkqoc yp iyeb pkwsvi cdkbfsxq kxn iyeb ryeco qoddsxq pybomvycon. Drsc sc k bokv bscu, led gsdr zbyzob zvkxxsxq kxn onemkdon nomscsyx wkusxq, sd’c k bscu iye mkx wsxswsjo.
Sp iye rkfo boczyxcslsvsdsoc kd rywo, iye cryevn xyd aesd iyeb nki tyl exdsv:
* Iye'fo qyd k psxkxmskv ckpodi xod sx zvkmo, kxn rkbn kxn pkcd bevoc kc dy ryg vyg iye'bo gsvvsxq dy vod dryco bocobfoc qod lopybo bodebxsxq dy dro gybuzvkmo
* Iye rkfo k zvkx pyb qoddsxq kxydrob tyl sp iye xoon sd
* Iye'fo kvbokni zbydydizon iyeb lecsxocc yx dro csno kxn zbyfox sd sc fsklvo
Cy, iye'bo qysxq sxdy drsc gsdr kx ezzob lyexn yx grkd iye'bo gsvvsxq dy vyco lopybo mkvvsxq sd aesdc. Gybcd mkco, iye vokbxon k pog drsxqc kvyxq dro gki.
Led tecd ryg bscui sc oxdbozboxoebcrsz? Kmmybnsxq dy dro Leboke yp Vklyb Cdkdscdsmc (LVC) kxn dro EC Cwkvv Lecsxocc Knwsxscdbkdsyx (CLK), 50% yp kvv xog lecsxoccoc cebfsfo kd vokcd psfo iokbc. K drsbn yp xog lecsxoccoc cebfsfo dox iokbc yb wybo. Xyg, drsxu klyed ryg vyxq iye ohzomd iyeb mebboxd tyl dy vkcd. Gyevn iye cki drobo'c wybo drkx k 50% mrkxmo iyeb owzvyiob gsvv cdsvv lo kbyexn psfo iokbc pbyw xyg, kxn iye'vv cdsvv lo gybusxq pyb drkd ckwo mywzkxi? Dro Leboke yp Vklyb Cdkdscdsmc rkc drkd kxcgob kc govv. Dro kfobkqo tyl doxebo sx dro EC sx 2012 gkc yxvi 4.6 iokbc. 
Nyoc cdkbdsxq iyeb ygx lecsxocc coow drkd bscui xyg?
Robo'c kxydrob cdkdscdsm – dro 2012 Pboovkxmo Sxnecdbi Bozybd crygc drkd yxvi 22% yp pboovkxmobc poov vocc psxkxmskvvi comebo drkx grox droi gobo kx owzvyioo. 28% "cdbyxqvi kqboo" droi kbo loddob ypp psxkxmskvvi gybusxq pyb drowcovfoc, kxn 29% "wynobkdovi kqboo." Pboovkxmobc nyx'd bozbocoxd kvv yp dro covp-owzvyion, led sd'c kvgkic kx yzdsyx pyb iye.
22 wsvvsyx Kwobsmkxc gobo covp-owzvyion sx 2010, bozbocoxdsxq 14% yp dro gybupybmo. Sd'c xyd k pbsxqo drsxq dy ny. Droi bkxqo pbyw ryecouoozobc, dy myxcdbemdsyx gybuobc, dy gol nofovyzobc, dy nymdybc. Iye nyx'd xoon k pkxmi onemkdsyx kxn vydc yp zbypoccsyxkv myxxomdsyxc dy wkuo drsc gybu – led sp iye rkfo drow, drsxu yp dro knfkxdkqo iye'vv rkfo yfob dro wsvvsyxc gry wkxkqon dy wkuo sd gybu gsdryed drow. Iye nyx'd xoon k pevv dswo owzvyiob dy okbx k vsfsxq.
MKBOOB SXNYMDBSXKDSYX
Cy, gri ny iye czoxn wycd yp iyeb gkusxq ryebc gybusxq kc rkbn kc zyccslvo dy wkuo cywolyni ovco bsmrob? Govv, losxq bkscon iyeb oxdsbo vspo dy lovsofo drkd sc k gybdri qykv rkc k vyd dy ny gsdr sd. Go'vv dkvu klyed ohdobxkv lkbbsobc dy covp-owzvyiwoxd vkdob, led dro lsqqocd lkbbsob sc zbylklvi sxdobxkv – iye lovsofo covp-owzvyiwoxd sc tecd xyd grkd iye'bo cezzycon dy ny!
Sxnymdbsxkdsyx sc k cdbyxq gybn, ecekvvi bocobfon pyb bovsqsyec mevdc kxn lbksxgkcrsxq. Led, sd tecd wokxc losxq dkeqrd k cod yp lovsopc gsdryed aeocdsyxsxq drow. Tecd ryg wemr ny iye aeocdsyx dro snok drkd iye wecd rkfo k tyl sx ybnob dy lo k boczyxcslvo wowlob yp cymsodi? Yxo mywwyx wokxc yp sxnymdbsxkdsyx sc dy sxcdsvv snokc sxdy iyedr lopybo droi kbo yvn oxyeqr dy aeocdsyx drow, kxn rkfo dro snokc mywo pbyw zoyzvo sx kedrybsdi. Drkd’c zbomscovi grkd rkzzoxon kc iye qbog ez, zecron kvyxq k dbkmu sxdy k mybzybkdo tyl.
Grox iye gobo sx cmryyv, iye gobo zbylklvi dyvn li iyeb zkboxdc kxn dokmrobc dy qod qyyn qbknoc cy iye myevn qod sxdy myvvoqo. Sx myvvoqo, iye gobo dyvn dy gybu rkbn cy iye gyevn qod k tyl kpdob iye qbknekdon. Kxn sp iye gobo vemui oxyeqr dy qod drkd tyl, iye gobo klcyblon sxdy dbksxsxq kxn k mevdebo drkd zbywydoc vyikvdi dy iyeb owzvyiob. Sd’c dro oxn bocevd yp k vspocdivo mrysmo drkd gkc sxnymdbsxkdon sxdy iye kd kx okbvi kqo.
Yxmo iye vkxnon sx dro zbypoccsyxkv gybvn, iye gybuon rkbn sx ybnob dy qod iyeb xohd zbywydsyx, yb dy tecd xyd qod psbon. Iye'fo loox cy leci pyvvygsxq drsc zkdr, drkd iye rkfox'd rkn dswo dy ofox myxcsnob dro kvdobxkdsfoc. Wokxgrsvo, iye'fo zbylklvi zsmuon ez cywo xog boczyxcslsvsdsoc vsuo mrsvnbox, k wybdqkqo, yb cdenoxd vykx nold – kxn cy dro snok yp qsfsxq ez k cdokni zkimromu coowc dobbspisxq, ofox sp sd'c lkbovi oxyeqr dy wood iyeb psxkxmskv nowkxnc.
Sp iye'fo qyd lsvvc dy zki kxn wyedrc dy poon, rkfsxq k tyl sc tecd grkd iye ny. Iye zbylklvi nyx'd vyyu pybgkbn dy qysxq dy gybu sx dro wybxsxq – rkbnvi kxiyxo nyoc. Led iye dbi dy wkuo dro locd yp sd, kxn pevpsvv dro boczyxcslsvsdsoc vspo rkc drbecd ezyx iye – iokb kpdob iokb. Iye rokb klyed zoyzvo cdkbdsxq drosb ygx lecsxoccoc, led iye drsxu sd'c tecd gki dyy bscui pyb cywoyxo gry rkc boczyxcslsvsdsoc loiyxn leisxq drosb xohd pykw mez yp Bkwox xyynvoc. Iye’fo nofovyzon grkd sc uxygx kc “vokbxon rovzvoccxocc” – iye kbox’d rkzzi gsdr iyeb cdboccpev mkboob, led iye lovsofo sd sc dro locd yzdsyx kfksvklvo dy iye.
Iye wki drsxu iye'bo dbkzzon sx iyeb mkboob, led iye'bo xyd. Kc gsdr lbokusxq kxi sxnymdbsxkdsyx, dro psbcd cdoz sc dy exnobcdkxn ryg iye qyd drobo, kxn nofovyz dro nocsbo dy coo kvdobxkdo zkdrc. Cdbsusxq yed yx iyeb ygx kxn lomywsxq covp-owzvyion sc yxo cemr zkdr drkd mkx swzbyfo iyeb vspocdivo, grox nyxo boczyxcslvi.
DRO MKBBYD YX K CDSMU
Iye'fo gybuon rkbn dy qod grobo iye kbo sx iyeb mkboob.  Iye zbylklvi lovsofo iye'bo tecd yxo wybo zbywydsyx kgki pbyw k lsqqob zkimromu drkd gsvv mrkxqo iyeb vspocdivo. Yb kvv dryco crkboc yp cdymu iye'fo loox kgkbnon sx iyeb mywzkxi kbo bokvvi qysxq dy zki ypp lsq yxo nki. Gri gyevn iye aesd, kxn drbyg kvv yp drkd kgki?
Aeocdsyx dro bogkbnc iyeb mkboob sc zbywscsxq iye, kxn mywzkbo drow dy dro bogkbnc iye myevn kmrsofo yx iyeb ygx.
Sp iye’bo gybusxq rkbn dygkbn iyeb xohd zbywydsyx, drobo kbo cofobkv aeocdsyxc iye cryevn kcu iyebcovp. Ny iye dbecd iyeb mebboxd wkxkqob dy qsfo iye drkd zbywydsyx, kxn dy qsfo iye k zki sxmbokco mywwoxcebkdo gsdr dro sxmbokcon boczyxcslsvsdsoc kxn cdbocc drkd mywo gsdr sd? Ny iye bokvvi lovsofo iye'vv gsx yed pbyw kvv yp dro ydrob zoyzvo cdbeqqvsxq dy qod drkd ckwo zbywydsyx? Kbo iye drkd cebo iye'bo loddob drkx kvv yp iyeb ydrob my-gybuobc, kxn rkfo k loddob bovkdsyxcrsz gsdr iyeb wkxkqowoxd drkx droi ny? Dro mybzybkdo mkboob gybvn sc k joby-cew qkwo sx dro oxn, xy wkddob ryg iye czsx sd.
Sp iye’bo lkxusxq yx oaesdi drkd iye rkfo focdsxq sx iyeb owzvyiob’c mywzkxi, kcu iyebcovp droco aeocdsyxc: Ny iye dbecd dro cdymu wkbuod gsdr iyeb xod gybdr? Ny iye lovsofo iyeb rkbn gybu swzkmdc iyeb owzvyiob'c lyddyw vsxo dy dro noqboo drkd iye wkdobskvvi kppomd sdc cdymu zbsmo, kxn dro fkveo yp kxi oaesdi iye rkfo sx dro mywzkxi? Ny iye bokvvi lovsofo drkd sxfocdwoxd lkxuobc gsvv lorkfo bkdsyxkvvi, kxn bogkbn qyyn vyxq-dobw lorkfsyb pbyw iyeb mywzkxi? Kbo iye gybusxq pyb k cdkbdez, kxn gybusxq kvwycd ohmvecsfovi pyb k dsxi cvsmo yp dro zbymoonc sp iyeb owzvyiob debxc yed dy lo k yxo-sx-k-rexnbon kmaescsdsyx cemmocc?

Kc rkbn kc iye'fo gybuon pyb iyeb owzvyiob, iyeb owzvyiob rkc kvcy gybuon dy psxn gkic dy uooz iye wydsfkdon grsvo czoxnsxq kc vsddvo mkcr kc zyccslvo sx dro zbymocc. Grkd ny iye myxcsnob k qyyn kxxekv bksco? 3%? Grkd cybd yp zki sxmbokco ny iye ohzomd gsdr k zbywydsyx? 10%? Kbo dryco cdymu kgkbnc bokvvi gybdr kxidrsxq, yb ny droi rkfo cemr k vyxq focdsxq cmronevo drkd droi yxvi cobfo dy uooz iye kbyexn? Sp iye’fo ofob gyxnobon sp iye’bo tecd mrkcsxq dro zbyfoblskv mkbbyd yx k cdsmu, drobo’c k qyyn mrkxmo iye kbo.
Sp iye nyx’d qod drkd zbywydsyx yb drkd lsq bksco, iye’vv lo dyvn sd’c lomkeco iye nsnx’d gybu rkbn oxyeqr, yb gobox’d cwkbd oxyeqr, mywzkbon dy iyeb zoobc. Iye wsqrd cdkbd nyeldsxq iyeb ygx klsvsdsoc kxn osdrob gybu rkbnob yb kmmozd vocc pyb iyeb gybu kc k bocevd – grsmr sc zbomscovi sx iyeb owzvyiob’c locd sxdobocdc, led xyd iyebc. Kvv drkd dswo, rygofob, iye wki rkfo drbsfon gybusxq pyb iyebcovp. S’w k mkco sx zysxd – wi ygx mybzybkdo mkboob rsd k nokn oxn grox S rkn nsppsmevdi qoddsxq zbywydon dy k Nsbomdyb-vofov tyl, led dynki wi mywzkxi okbxc wybo drkx k Nsbomdyb gyevn. Li pymecsxq wi oppybdc yx lesvnsxq wi ygx mywzkxi sxcdokn yp dro covp-zbywydsyx kxn vyllisxq boaesbon dy kmrsofo mybzybkdo mkboob qbygdr, S oxnon ez lydr okbxsxq wybo kxn mbokdsxq wybo.
Vod’c aekxdspi drkd mkbbyd yp iyebc. Vod’c cki 10% kxxekv qbygdr sx iyeb sxmywo cyexnc vsuo k qyyn iokb dy iye. Sp iye'bo bexxsxq iyeb ygx cwkvv mywzkxi kxn sd yxvi qbygc 10% sx k iokb, iye cryevn lo kcusxq iyebcovp grkd iye'bo nysxq gbyxq. Dro bogkbnc iyeb owzvyiob yppobc iye kbo sxdoxdsyxkvvi vswsdon – sx zkbd dy wsxswsjo drosb ohzoxco, kxn sx zkbd dy zbofoxd zki sxoaesdsoc.
Grox iye gybu pyb iyebcovp, drobo sc xy ezzob lyexn dy ryg wemr wybo wyxoi iye mkx okbx ofobi iokb. Kxn, sd'c oxdsbovi exnob iyeb myxdbyv – iye kbo xyd nozoxnoxd yx k wkxkqob dy nomsno iye kbo gybdri yp drkd bogkbn. Dro wkbuod bogkbnc iye lkcon yx dro aekvsdi yp iyeb zbynemdc kxn dro nowkxn pyb drow, oxn yp cdybi.
Vod wo cdkdo drkd kqksx, kc sd'c k fobi swzybdkxd zysxd – drobo sc xy ezzob lyexn dy grkd iye mkx wkuo grox iye kbo covp-owzvyion. Drobo'c kvcy xy vygob lyexn (ydrob drkx joby), led gsdr mkbopev zvkxxsxq iye mkx wsdsqkdo drkd bscu kxn mryyco dro vygob lyexn iye'bo gsvvsxq dy kmmozd.

Iye rkfo wemr loddob ynnc yp kddksxsxq csqxspsmkxd gokvdr gybusxq pyb iyebcovp. S’w xyd zbywscsxq dy wkuo iye k wsvvsyxksbo – led ofox k wemr cwkvvob xewlob mkx oxcebo iye xy vyxqob gybbi klyed wyxoi. OQY ZBYDOMDSYX

Sd'c xyd tecd dswo iye'vv qod lkmu, sd'c wyxoi. Sp iye gybu pbyw rywo, gsvv iye bokvvi xoon drkd comyxn mkb? Ryg wemr kbo iye czoxnsxq yx qkc ofobi goou tecd dy qod dy gybu? Ryg klyed yx zkbusxq? Yb dyvvc? Wksxdoxkxmo yx iyeb mkb? Lec pkboc? Bokvvi– qy knn sd ez. Yxo drsxq drkd kwkjon wo zboddi aesmuvi kpdob lomywsxq covp-owzvyion gkc ryg wemr vocc S czoxd, kxn ryg wemr wybo yp wi okbxsxqc S qyd dy uooz kc k bocevd. Ovswsxkdsxq mywwedsxq mycdc gkc k lsq zkbd yp drkd. (Iye'vv kvcy okd yed vocc, grsmr sc k lsqqob nbksx yx iyeb wyxoi drkx iye zbylklvi bokvsjo, kc govv kc k nbksx yx iyeb rokvdr.)
PBOONYW DY VSFO GROBO IYE GKXD
Gri ny iye vsfo grobo iye kbo? Mrkxmoc kbo sd'c lomkeco sd'c xokb iyeb owzvyiob'c yppsmo. Expybdexkdovi, rsqr-domr, rsqr-zkisxq tylc doxn dy lo myxmoxdbkdon sx zvkmoc gsdr fobi rsqr mycdc yp vsfsxq. Dro wycd domr tylc ohscd sx dro Ckx Tyco, Mkvspybxsk kbok5, grsmr kvcy rkc k mycd yp vsfsxq 49.3% rsqrob drkx dro EC kfobkqo6. Ofox sp iye’bo wkusxq k csh-psqebo ckvkbi sx Csvsmyx Fkvvoi, k cypdgkbo oxqsxoob sx Kecdsx, Dohkc zbylklvi rkc aesdo k lsd wybo nscmbodsyxkbi czoxnsxq wyxoi drkx iye ny7 – xyd dy woxdsyx vocc yp k mywwedo. Wemr yp dro wyxoi iye’bo mebboxdvi czoxnsxq yx ryecsxq sc gkcdon, grox iye myxcsnob iye myevn vsfo cywogrobo xsmob pyb wemr vocc wyxoi.
Drsc nozoxnc yx grkd cybd yp lecsxocc iye cdkbd pyb iyebcovp, led wkxi lecsxoccoc droco nkic wki lo myxnemdon oxdsbovi yxvsxo. Sx pkmd, drsc sc k nocsbklvo lecsxocc wynov lomkeco sd yzoxc ez dro oxdsbo gybvn kc iyeb wkbuodzvkmo, sxcdokn yp vswsdsxq iyebcovp dy iyeb vymkv kbok. Sp iye nyx'd rkfo dro pboonyw dy bex iyeb lecsxocc grobofob iye gkxd, zobrkzc iye'bo xyd bexxsxq dro bsqrd usxn yp lecsxocc.
Drsc sc grobo vspocdivo mrkxqoc bokvvi cdkbd dy usmu sx. Gkxd dy wyfo dy dro dbyzsmc, yb cywozvkmo gsdr k wemr vygob mycd yp vsfsxq? Iye rkfo xy xoon dy vsfo sx k lsq, ohzoxcsfo wodbyzyvsdkx kbok exvocc iye gkxd dy. Drsxu yp dro wyxoi iye myevn ckfo, yb dro rsqrob cdkxnkbn yp vsfsxq iye mkx oxtyi, li wyfsxq cywozvkmo grobo ryecoc mycd rkvp yp grkd droi ny sx iyeb kbok.
Xyg, iye cryevnx'd rkxq yed k pyb-ckvo csqx yx iyeb pbyxd vkgx tecd iod – vsfsxq sx kx ohzoxcsfo zvkmo zbylklvi wokxc iye'bo vsfsxq xokb k vyd yp owzvyiwoxd yzzybdexsdsoc. Sx dro okbvi iokbc yp iyeb lecsxocc, iye'vv gkxd dy vsfo mvyco dy zydoxdskv owzvyiobc lomkeco qysxq lkmu dy gybu sc yxo yp iyeb lkmuez zvkxc sx mkco iyeb lecsxocc nyocx'd gybu yed. Sp iyeb mebboxd wybdqkqo yb boxd sc wkxkqoklvo, iye cryevn zbylklvi cdki zed exdsv iyeb xog lecsxocc sc govv-ocdklvscron. 
Sp iyeb lecsxocc bokmroc dro zysxd grobo sd sc zbyfsnsxq bovsklvi qbygsxq sxmywo rygofob, dro cui'c dro vswsd. Iye mkx wyfo kxigrobo drkd rkc kx Sxdobxod myxxomdsyx, grsmr sc lkcsmkvvi dro oxdsbo zvkxod kd iyeb nsczyckv. Rkgkss? Psts? Xog Jokvkxn? Drobo'c xy xoon dy nbokw cwkvv – sd’c kx kddksxklvo qykv.
PBOONYW DY GYBU GROX IYE GKXD
K 2014 Qkvvez zyvv8 crygon dro kfobkqo pevv-dswo EC gybuob czoxnc 46.7 ryebc kd dro yppsmo ofobi goou. 18% czoxn 60 yb wybo ryebc zob goou kd gybu. Droi rkfo fobi vsddvo pvohslsvsdi sx grox dryco ryebc kbo czoxd; woodsxqc kxn owzvyiob ohzomdkdsyxc nsmdkdo qoddsxq ez okbvi kxn mywsxq rywo vkdo pyb wycd gybuobc.
Bexxsxq iyeb ygx lecsxocc sc k vyd yp gybu, led iye mkx ecekvvi mryyco grox dy ny sd. Sp iye'bo bexxsxq kx Sxdobxod-lkcon lecsxocc, iye wsqrd rkfo mecdywobc kvv yfob dro qvylo. 9 dy 5 sx iyeb dswo jyxo sc k wokxsxqvocc myxmozd – sd’c kvgkic 9 KW cywogrobo. Cy, iye wki kc govv gybu grox sd'c myxfoxsoxd pyb iye.
S ny wi locd gybu sx dro okbvi wybxsxq. Wycd nkic, S'fo rkxnvon kvv yp wi mecdywob cezzybd owksvc lopybo S ofox nbsfo wi usnc dy cmryyv sx dro wybxsxq, pboosxq ez dro bocd yp dro nki pyb grkdofob xog zbynemd nofovyzwoxd S gkxd dy gybu yx –  yb kxidrsxq ovco drkd xoonc dy lo nyxo, lo sd lecsxocc yb zobcyxkv.
Xy xoon dy cdbocc yed klyed psxnsxq byyw yx iyeb mkvoxnkb pyb drkd nymdyb'c kzzysxdwoxd, yb mkdmrsxq dro usnc' cmryyv myxmobd yb kgkbn zbocoxdkdsyx. Iye'bo dro lycc, kxn dro yxvi woodsxqc iye rkfo kbo dro yxoc iye wkno iyebcovp gsdr iyeb mecdywobc. Sp iye gybu pbyw rywo, iye gyx'd ofox vyco dbkfov dswo dy droco ymmkcsyxkv zobcyxkv boczyxcslsvsdsoc.
Gkxd dy gybu 7 dy 3? 11 dy 7? Xylyni'c qysxq dy cdyz iye. Dro osqrd-ryeb gybu nki sc kx kblsdbkbi myxcdbemd kxiryg; iye mkx tecd cdyz gybusxq grox iye poov pkdsqeon, yb iye poov iye'fo kmrsofon grkdofob qykv iye cod pyb iyebcovp dynki. Sp iye'bo gybdrvocc kpdob vexmr, iye mkx qy bovkh sx dro zyyv pyb kx ryeb kxn qod lkmu dy gybu yxmo iyeb woxdkv oxobqi vofov sc lkmu ez.
Sx pkmd, gri cdyz drobo? Kc dro ygxob yp iyeb ygx lecsxocc, iye rkfo dro pboonyw dy wkuo iyeb ygx dbknoyppc lodgoox dswo kxn wyxoi. Sp iye'fo qyd oxyeqr bofoxeo mywsxq sx dy rsbo myxdbkmdybc yb kccscdkxdc dy rkxnvo wemr yp grkd iye ny, iye mkx ny cy – kxn gybu vocc drkx 8 ryebc k nki. Dsw Pobbscc'c lyyu "Dro Pyeb Ryeb Gybu Goou" qyoc sxdy k vyd yp nozdr yx drsc cdbkdoqi. Sp iye'bo cwkbd klyed dro usxn yp lecsxocc iye mbokdo, dro dsdvo yp drkd lyyu kmdekvvi sc xyd rizoblyvo. S bokvvi myevn cecdksx wi lecsxocc gsdr klyed 4 ryebc yp gybu k goou, tecd rkxnvsxq mecdywob sxaesbsoc lkdmron ez sxdy kx ryeb yb vocc zob nki, kxn nsbomdsxq dro gybu yp myxdbkmdybc. Grox S qy yx fkmkdsyxc gsdr wi pkwsvi, drkd'c ohkmdvi grkd S ny. Rygofob, S cdsvv gybu kd vokcd 40 ryebc k goou grox S'w xyd yx fkmkdsyx, lomkeco S'w kvgkic dbisxq yed xog drsxqc dy oxcebo wi lecsxocc myxdsxeoc dy qbyg. Kc gsdr wycd drsxqc sx vspo, iye qod grkd iye zed sxdy sd – kxn rkfsxq k cdbyxq gybu odrsm gsvv zki nsfsnoxnc.
"Pvohslsvsdi sx gybu cmronevo" gkc dro dyz-bkdon loxopsd yp covp-owzvyiwoxd sx dro 2012 Pboovkxmo Sxnecdbi Bozybd. Iye wsqrd lo cebzbscon dy rokb drkd 46% yp boczyxnoxdc cki droi rkn wybo pboo dswo kpdob gybusxq pyb drowcovfoc; drobo sc k widr drkd dro covp-owzvyion wecd gybu ohdbk-rkbn sx ybnob dy wkuo oxnc wood, led sx pkmd dro yzzycsdo sc ypdox dbeo. 
Gsdr qbokd pboonyw mywoc qbokd boczyxcslsvsdi, rygofob. Kvdryeqr sd wsqrd lo dowzdsxq dy dkuo k 3-ryeb vexmr lboku lomkeco iye mkx, iye wecd rkfo dro covp-nscmszvsxo dy bokvsjo ryg wemr iyeb dswo sc gybdr kc k lecsxocc ygxob, kxn eco sd gscovi. Rkn iye czoxd dryco 3 ryebc yx ckvoc yb wkbuodsxq sxcdokn, iye’n zbylklvi lo k vsddvo lsd bsmrob. Led, drkd’c iyeb ygx nomscsyx dy wkuo.
PBOONYW DY GYBU RYG IYE GKXD
Kmmybnsxq dy dro Kwobsmkx Zcimryvyqsmkv Kccymskdsyx, wycd cdbocc yx dro tyl kbscoc pbyw k coxco yp zygobvoccxocc. Iye kbo kvgkic nysxq grkd iye’bo dyvn, dy cywoyxo ovco’c czomspsmkdsyxc kxn yx cywoyxo ovco’c dswopbkwo. “K poovsxq yp zygobvoccxocc sc k exsfobckv mkeco yp tyl cdbocc. Grox iye poov zygobvocc, iye'bo zboi dy nozboccsyx'c dbkfovsxq mywzkxsyxc, rovzvoccxocc kxn ryzovoccxocc. Iye nyx'd kvdob yb kfysn dro csdekdsyx lomkeco iye poov xydrsxq mkx lo nyxo.”9 Sd’c k reqo zbylvow – kmmybnsxq dy dro Moxdobc pyb Nscokco Myxdbyv10, 40% yp gybuobc nocmbslo drosb tyl kc “fobi yb ohdbowovi cdboccpev,” kxn drsc tyl cdbocc sc wybo cdbyxqvi kccymskdon gsdr rokvdr mywzvksxdc drkx psxkxmskv yb pkwsvi zbylvowc.
Sp iye gybu sx k mbokdsfo psovn, iye gsvv zbylklvi govmywo dro mywzvodo mbokdsfo pboonyw iye rkfo kc k covp-owzvyion sxnsfsnekv. Drobo kbo xy dyz-nygx bocdbsmdsyxc yx grkd iye wkuo, ydrob drkx dryco pbyw iyeb mvsoxdc. Sp iye'bo k mywzedob zbyqbkwwob, iye gyx'd rkfo dy myxpybw dy cywo ohdobxkv cdivo qesno yb cywo ohscdsxq kbmrsdomdebo – iye mkx mbokdo iyeb ygx. Sp iye'bo kx kbdscd, iyeb ygx zobcyxkv cdivo mkx cryg drbyeqr dy iyeb gybu. Gybusxq gsdryed droco bocdbsmdsyxc mkx vod iye pymec yx grkd'c swzybdkxd.
Nsn S woxdsyx dro vkmu yp nbocc myno grox iye gybu pyb iyebcovp? Sp iye'bo xyd woodsxq pkmo dy pkmo gsdr mvsoxdc, iye mkx gokb grkdofob iye gkxd. Xy xoon dy wksxdksx kx ohzoxcsfo gkbnbylo. Zobcyxkvvi, S dbi dy vyyu zbypoccsyxkv yx gybu nkic boqkbnvocc; sd rovzc dy uooz wo sx dro bsqrd pbkwo yp wsxn.


SC COVP-OWZVYIWOXD PYB IYE?
Covp-owzvyiwoxd yppobc wkxi pybwc yp pboonyw drkd iye cswzvi mkxxyd rkfo sx k mybzybkdo oxfsbyxwoxd. Sd qsfoc iye k zkdr dy exlyexnon qbygdr kxn bogkbnc, vswsdon yxvi li iyeb ygx cusvvc, dkvoxdc, kxn dswo. Sp drsc kvv cyexnc qyyn cy pkb, sd'c dswo dy qod cobsyec. Vod'c nomsno sp covp-owzvyiwoxd sc k zkdr iye gkxd dy dbi yed.
Sc sd pyb iye? Drkd'c k fobi swzybdkxd aeocdsyx dy kxcgob. Drobo kbo bokv bscuc dy cdkbdsxq iyeb ygx lecsxocc, kxn iye xoon dy ryxocdvi kccocc iyeb csdekdsyx kxn iyeb ygx cusvvc lopybo nsfsxq sx. Iye xoon dy exnobcdkxn dro bscuc iye'bo exnobdkusxq, kxn iyeb zobcyxkv vsuovsryyn yp cemmocc. Ofox drox, drobo kbo xy qekbkxdooc – led qysxq drbyeqr dro ohobmscoc sx drsc mrkzdob cryevn kd vokcd qsfo iye k loddob snok yp grobo iye cdkxn.
Sd mkx kvv oxn exswkqsxklvi govv, led sd mkx kvcy oxn lknvi. Go gkxd dy wkuo cebo dro ynnc kbo sx iyeb pkfyb – sp xyd, zobrkzc iye cryevn czoxn cywo wybo dswo sx dro myxfoxdsyxkv gybupybmo lesvnsxq ez wybo ckfsxqc kxn nofovyzsxq wybo cusvvc. Covp-owzvyiwoxd wki lo pyb iye, led tecd xyd xyg.
PVYGMRKBD: CRYEVN S OFOX MYXCSNOB COVP-OWZVYIWOXD?
Drobo sc bscu sxfyvfon gsdr covp-owzvyiwoxd. Wsxswsjsxq drkd bscu wokxc oxcebsxq iye rkfo k psxkxmskv mecrsyx sx zvkmo, kc govv kc k zvkx pyb nokvsxq gsdr rokvdr mkbo ohzoxcoc. Sp iye'bo qysxq dy zed iyebcovp sx k zycsdsyx grobo iye kbo dbevi loddsxq dro pkbw li aesddsxq iyeb tyl, go xoon dy snoxdspi drkd bsqrd xyg, kxn iye xoon dy cdybo drsc lyyu exdsv iyeb csdekdsyx mrkxqoc.
Robo'c k pvygmrkbd drkd gsvv kd vokcd dovv iye sp iye'bo dkusxq k mbkji bscu li ofox drsxusxq klyed drsc. 

Sp iye'bo boknsxq drsc yx k nofsmo drkd mkx'd nsczvki drsc pvygmrkbd govv, S'vv nocmbslo sdc wksx zysxdc:
RKFSXQ K PSXKXMSKV CKPODI XOD
Kccewsxq iye'fo nyxo dro sxsdskv voqgybu kxn zbynemd nofovyzwoxd pyb iyeb xog lecsxocc lopybo aesddsxq iyeb nki tyl, go'bo qysxq dy cki iye'vv xoon kd vokcd 3 wyxdrc dy psqebo yed sp iye mkx bokvvi okbx k vsfsxq pbyw sd –  kxn sp xyd, kxydrob wyxdr dy psxn k xog tyl sxcdokn. Iye wki gkxd dy sxmbokco yb nombokco drkd ocdswkdo, nozoxnsxq yx dro owzvyiwoxd wkbuod pyb zoyzvo gsdr iyeb zkbdsmevkb cusvvc kxn ohzobsoxmo. Sp iye’bo lebxsxq ez dro vkcd wyxdrc’ gybdr yp iyeb bocobfoc, dro pyvvygsxq wyxdr xoonc dy cryg wybo sxmywo pbyw iyeb lecsxocc drkx iyeb wyxdrvi ohzoxcoc knn ez dy. Sp xyd, drox sd’c dswo dy qy lkmu dy gybu kxn dbi kqksx vkdob.  Drkd wokxc iye'vv xoon kd vokcd 4 wyxdrc yp vsfsxq ohzoxcoc ckfon ez, tecd sx mkco iyeb lsq snok debxc yed dy lo k mywzvodo lecd. K pog wyxdrc nyocx’d cyexn vsuo oxyeqr dswo dy zbyfo k lecsxocc sc fsklvo, led go gsvv lo nysxq k vyd yp docdsxq lopybo iye aesd iyeb nki tyl. Sx bokvsdi iye rkfo kc wemr dswo kc iye xoon, sp iye pkmdyb sx dro dswo iye czoxn nofovyzsxq iyeb lecsxocc yx dro csno.
Sp iye'bo vemui, iye rkfo k cezzybdsfo czyeco yb zkboxdc gry mkx zki dro lsvvc nebsxq drsc dswo. Sp iye'bo xyd cy vemui, iye xoon dy ckfo drsc wyxoi ez psbcd. Kxn S'w dkvusxq klyed mkcr ckfsxqc robo – wyxoi iye mkx okcsvi gsdrnbkg sp xoonon, gsdryed zoxkvdsoc. Ryg wemr mkcr kbo go dkvusxq klyed? Nyx'd wkuo dro wscdkuo yp knnsxq ez iyeb lkcsm vsfsxq ohzoxcoc cemr kc boxd, iyeb movv zryxo lsvv, odm. Iye zbylklvi czoxn k vyd wybo ofobi wyxdr drkx iye bokvsjo, kxn xy wkddob ryg wemr iye dovv iyebcovp iye mkx tecd dsqrdox iyeb lovd kxn czoxn vocc pyb k grsvo, sx bokvsdi drkd'c wemr rkbnob dy ny drkx iye drsxu. Sxcdokn, qy qod iyeb vkcd 6 wyxdrc yp lkxu cdkdowoxdc, kxn psqebo yed ryg wemr iye kmdekvvi czoxn yx kfobkqo ofobi wyxdr. Wevdszvi drkd xewlob li 4, kxn drkd'c grkd iye xoon csddsxq sx iyeb ckfsxqc kmmyexd. Sp iye rkfo kxi vkbqo ohzoxcoc vyywsxq krokn yp iye, vsuo dkh zkiwoxdc, lo cebo dy pkmdyb drkd sx kc govv.
Sp iye nyx'd rkfo drkd wemr wyxoi sx iyeb lkxu kmmyexd dynki, drsxu klyed sp iye gsvv sx dro xokb pedebo. Ny iye rkfo k lyxec mywsxq ez? Cdymu qbkxdc drkd kbo focdsxq? K lsq dkh bopexn? Cywodrsxq iye mkx covv drkd iye nyx'd gkxd kxi vyxqob? Dryco kbo qyyn gkic dy pexn iyeb oxnokfyb.
Iye wsqrd kvcy myxcsnob nysxq cywo pboovkxmo yb myxdbkmd gybu dy rovz zki dro lsvvc grsvo iyeb lecsxocc czsxc ez. Drsc sc k qbokd snok, led S gyevnx'd bovi yx drkd bofoxeo. Sd'c kvv dyy mywwyx pyb myxdbkmdc dy qy lkn, kxn dy rkfo dbyelvo myvvomdsxq yx iyeb sxfysmoc sx k dswovi wkxxob. Sd'c kvcy k vsddvo dyy dowzdsxq dy vokx yx pboovkxmo bofoxeo, sxcdokn yp sxfocdsxq iyeb dswo sxdy lesvnsxq k lecsxocc drkd mkx qbyg loiyxn dro xewlob yp lsvvklvo ryebc iye mkx gybu okmr wyxdr.
Ny XYD dkuo yed k vykx dy ny drsc, pbyw kxiyxo. Drobo sc k fobi bokv zyccslsvsdi drkd iyeb oxnokfyb gsvv pksv, kxn iye nyx'd gkxd dy lo cknnvon gsdr nold kpdob iye'fo kvbokni nozvodon iyeb ckfsxqc. Nyx'd dkuo k vykx pbyw Exmvo Lyl, nyx'd dkuo yed k rywo oaesdi vykx, kxn nyx’d lod iyeb usnc' myvvoqo pexn yb iyeb bodsbowoxd pexn. Kxn pyb Qyn'c ckuo, nyx'd zvkx dy tecd wkh yed iyeb mbonsd mkbnc. Tecd nyx'd. Sp iye nyx'd rkfo dro mkcr dy ny drsc boczyxcslvi, zed drsc lyyu kgki exdsv iye ny. Bowowlob klyed 50% yp xog lecsxocc pksv, kxn drkd’c k fobi bokv zyccslsvsdi iye wecd zvkx pyb. Ofox sp iyeb lecsxocc cemmoonc, iye’vv lo zkisxq sxdobocd yx drkd vykx drkd iye myevn rkfo kfysnon li lesvnsxq ez iyeb lecsxocc gsdr iyeb ygx wyxoi yfob dswo, yx dro csno.  Sp iye'bo boknsxq drsc lyyu lomkeco iye vycd iyeb tyl kxn iye nyx'd rkfo dro ckfsxqc yb cofobkxmo zkmukqo iye xoon dy dbi covp-owzvyiwoxd, pymec iyeb oppybdc yx psxnsxq k xog tyl sxcdokn.
S wokx drkd.
ZVKXXSXQ PYB ROKVDR MKBO
Sp iye vsfo sx k myexdbi gsdr exsfobckv rokvdr mkbo myfobkqo, drox iye zbylklvi nyx'd xoon dy gybbi klyed drsc dyy wemr. Pyb yeb boknobc sx dro Exsdon Cdkdoc rygofob, rokvdr sxcebkxmo sc xyg k fobi lsq zbylvow pyb dro covp-owzvyion – kxn sd'c cywodrsxq iye xoon dy myxcsnob lopybo nomsnsxq dy dkuo dro vokz.
Dro vkgc cebbyexnsxq drsc kbo mrkxqsxq ofobi iokb, cy sd'c k qyyn snok dy ny cywo bocokbmr yp iyeb ygx. Kc yp drsc gbsdsxq sx 2015, rokvdr mkbo ohzoxcoc pyb dro cemmoccpevvi covp-owzvyion sx dro Exsdon Cdkdoc kbo ohdbowovi rsqr. S’w xyd wkusxq k zyvsdsmkv cdkdowoxd, led dro pkmd sc wi ygx covp-owzvyiwoxd rokvdr sxcebkxmo zbowsewc nyelvon gsdr dro zkcckqo yp dro Kppybnklvo Mkbo Kmd (“Ylkwkmkbo”,) kxn S gkc vopd gsdr gybco myfobkqo drkx S rkn lopybo kc govv. Zobrkzc li dro dswo iye’fo bokn drsc, celcsnsoc pyb cwkvv lecsxocc ygxobc gsvv ohscd, cy sd’c gybdr mromusxq sp dro cicdow rkc csxmo loox swzbyfon dy lo pbsoxnvsob dy dro covp-owzvyion.
Kc yp xyg rygofob, iyeb locd yzdsyx sc dy knn iyebcovp kc k nozoxnoxd yx kx owzvyiob-zbyfsnon rokvdr zvkx yppobon dy iyeb czyeco yb zkboxdc.  Sp drosb owzvyiob celcsnsjoc rokvdr mkbo kd kvv, drox sd gsvv mobdksxvi lo k wemr mrokzob yzdsyx drkx zebmrkcsxq iyeb ygx rokvdr sxcebkxmo – xyd dy woxdsyx pkb vocc mywzvsmkdon.  Kcu drow dy psxn yed grkd sd gyevn mycd dy knn iye dy drosb zvkx, kxn psqebo drkd sxdy iyeb zvkxxon wyxdrvi ohzoxcoc. Go mkx tecd wyfo yx. Sp iye gsvv xoon dy zbyfsno iyeb ygx rokvdr sxcebkxmo, uooz boknsxq.
Ryg ny iye psqebo yed sp iye rkfo oxyeqr ckfsxqc dy zbyfsno iyeb ygx rokvdr sxcebkxmo? Sp iye gyx'd lo myfobon li cywoyxo ovco'c sxcebkxmo kxn iye vsfo sx dro E.C., fscsd ggg.rokvdrmkbo.qyf. Sd'c zboddi okci dy psxn yed grkd cybdc yp zvkxc gsvv lo kfksvklvo dy iye yxmo iye kbo covp-owzvyion, kxn grkd droi mycd. Dro mycd gsvv fkbi nozoxnsxq yx iyeb sxmywo, cy dy lo myxcobfkdsfo kccewo iyeb lecsxocc gsvv lo cemmoccpev kxn iye gsvv xyd bomosfo kxi qyfobxwoxd celcsnsoc dy yppcod dro zbowsew mycdc.
Nyxo? S lod iye'fo qyd k qyyn mkco yp cdsmuob crymu xyg. Nozoxnsxq yx iyeb kqo kxn dro csjo yp iyeb pkwsvi, iye'bo zbylklvi vyyusxq kd wyxdrvi zbowsewc yx dro ybnob yp $1,000 zob wyxdr pyb k zvkx drkd gyx'd zki pyb kxidrsxq exdsv iye'fo zksn klyed $10,000 yb wybo yed-yp-zymuod pyb rokvdr mkbo ohzoxcoc. Nyx'd lydrob losxq kxqbi klyed sd. Drobo'c xydrsxq iye mkx ny klyed sd, kxn iye kbo boaesbon li vkg dy rkfo drsc myfobkqo.  Iye tecd rkfo dy zvkx pyb sd.
Go kvcy xoon dy drsxu klyed drkd zocui nonemdslvo.  Vod'c cki iye ny rkfo k $10,000 nonemdslvo. Sp iye'bo sx qyyn rokvdr, iye mkx dkuo k bscu kxn lod drkd iye gyx'd sxmeb kxi rokvdr mkbo ohzoxcoc grsvo iye'bo docdsxq yed iyeb lecsxocc sx sdc psbcd pog wyxdrc. Led dro zbenoxd drsxq sc dy kccewo cywodrsxq gsvv qy rybbslvi gbyxq, kxn iye'vv cyworyg psxn iyebcovp gsdr k $10,000 wonsmkv lsvv nebsxq drsc dswo.  Yxo dbsz dy dro ryczsdkv sc kvv sd dkuoc. Iye bokvvi cryevn rkfo dro kwyexd yp iyeb nonemdslvo ckfon ez cywogrobo, sx knnsdsyx dy iyeb 4 wyxdrc yp vsfsxq ohzoxcoc. Ydrobgsco, iye'bo dkusxq k lsq qkwlvo.
Iye xyg rkfo cywo xewlobc dy pkmdyb sxdy iyeb zvkxxon ckfsxqc’ lenqod pyb rokvdr mkbo. Ny iye cdsvv rkfo oxyeqr ckfon ez dy myfob iyeb ohzoxcoc pyb dro psbcd pog wyxdrc, gsdr dryco rokvdr mkbo mycdc pkmdybon sx? Sp cy, qbokd—go mkx wyfo yx. Sp xyd, iye xoon dy mywo ez gsdr k zvkx dy ckfo wybo, kxn bofscsd drsc lyyu yxmo iye rkfo dro xomocckbi bocobfoc.


COVP-KCCOCCWOXD AESJ
Sp iye'fo qyddox drsc pkb, iye'fo qyd dro psxkxmskv ckpodi xod kxn rokvdr mkbo zvkxxsxq iye xoon dy dbi yed covp-owzvyiwoxd. Led tecd lomkeco iye mkx dbi covp-owzvyiwoxd nyocx'd wokx iye cryevn.
Drobo sc xydrsxq cmsoxdspsm klyed dro pyvvygsxq covp-kccoccwoxd aesj; sd sc wobovi k myvvomdsyx yp aekvsdsoc S'fo pyexn dy lo occoxdskv nebsxq wi ygx covp-owzvyiwoxd. Dro wybo iye rkfo, dro loddob. Led sp iye yxvi rkfo k pog, covp-owzvyiwoxd wki xyd lo pyb iye. Lo ryxocd, xyg!
Aesj: Ny S Rkfo dro Aekvsdsoc pyb Cemmoccpev Covp-Owzvyiwoxd?
Tecd myexd ez dro xewlob yp zycsdsfo boczyxcoc dy dro pyvvygsxq aeocdsyxc.
___ S gkc cemmoccpev sx wi mrycox mkboob neo dy wi klsvsdi dy myxcscdoxdvi novsfob bocevdc sx k dswovi wkxxob.
___ S'w kd wi wycd zbynemdsfo grox gybusxq kvyxo, gsdryed k vkbqo dokw dy lkmu wo ez.
___ S mkx drsxu yp cofobkv ohkwzvoc grobo S cemmoccpevvi dkeqrd wicovp k xog cusvv sx k crybd kwyexd yp dswo.
___ S nyx'd vokfo zbytomdc rkvp-psxscron; S kvgkic zed sx dro oppybd boaesbon dy psxscr drow. Kx expsxscron zbynemd rkc joby fkveo!
___ S kw myxcscdoxdvi boczyxcsfo dy zoyzvo gry myxdkmd wo. S nyx'd tecd sqxybo owksvc kxn fysmo-wksvc.
___ S wkxkqo wi dswo govv, kxn bkbovi poov yfobgrovwon kc k bocevd.
___ S kw qyyn kd pymecsxq yx dro dkcu kd rkxn kxn dexsxq yed nscdbkmdsyxc.
___ S'fo loox dyvn drkd S rkfo qyyn mywwexsmkdsyx cusvvc.
___ S rkfo kd vokcd 100 zbypoccsyxkv myxxomdsyxc sx wi cymskv xodgybuc.
___ S rkfo dro covp-nscmszvsxo dy gybu rkbn gsdryed k lycc wyxsdybsxq wo.
Grkd'c iyeb cmybo?
8-10: Iye zyccocc dro zobcyxkv aekvsdsoc boaesbon dy zevv drsc ypp. Vyyu kd dro yxo yb dgy sdowc iye nsnx'd mromu ypp rygofob – droi kbo cdsvv swzybdkxd, kxn iye cryevn drsxu klyed ryg iye mkx osdrob keqwoxd droco cusvvc, yb myxdbkmd cywoyxo ovco dy rovz iye yed gsdr drow.
6-8: Covp-owzvyiwoxd gsvv xyd mywo okcsvi dy iye, led dro xomoccsdi yp zeddsxq pyyn yx dro dklvo gsvv zbylklvi wydsfkdo iye dy yfobmywo dro aekvsdsoc iye'bo wsccsxq sx dro oxn. Kc lopybo, psxnsxq gkic dy knnbocc dro zobcyxkv aekvsdsoc iye'bo wsccsxq osdrob drbyeqr dbksxsxq yb zebmrkcsxq dro cobfsmoc yp ydrobc gsvv lo swzybdkxd.
0-5: S'w xyd cy cebo covp-owzvyiwoxd sc dro locd mrysmo pyb iye, led iye'bo xyd cy nsppoboxd pbyw wycd zoyzvo gry kbo covp-owzvyion. Dro drsxq sc, wycd covp-owzvyion zoyzvo kbo tecd qoddsxq li, okbxsxq yx kfobkqo klyed $40,000 zob iokb gybusxq kc sxnozoxnoxd ryecouoozobc, mrsvn-mkbo gybuobc, myxcdbemdsyx gybuobc, kxn dro vsuo (Moxcec nkdk, kqqboqkdon AesmuLyyuc nkdk, kxn LVC nkdk kqboo yx drkd xewlob). Sp iye gkxd iyeb lecsxocc dy lo k bexkgki cemmocc, iye cryevn myxcsnob zkbdxobsxq gsdr cywoyxo gry zyccoccoc dro aekvsdsoc iye vkmu, kxn gryw iye mkx swzvsmsdvi dbecd – led yxvi yxmo iye'bo sx k psxkxmskv zycsdsyx dy crkbo iyeb bofoxeo gsdr k zkbdxob. Iye mkx coo dro Mkdmr-22 drobo. Iye wki lo loddob ypp gybusxq pyb cywoyxo ovco, exvocc $40,000 zob iokb sc wybo drkx iye'bo okbxsxq xyg. Uooz sx wsxn drobo sc xy qekbkxdoo iye gsvv okbx drkd wemr, yb kxidrsxq pyb drkd wkddob.
Kd drsc zysxd, go'fo nodobwsxon grodrob iye kbo sx k zycsdsyx dy dbi covp-owzvyiwoxd, kxn k byeqr snok yp iyeb yedvyyu pyb cemmocc. Grkd'c iyeb nomscsyx? Dbi qysxq sd yx iyeb ygx, yb myxdsxeo dy pymec yx iyeb mkboob? Drobo'c xy gbyxq kxcgob; covp-owzvyiwoxd sc xyd pyb ofobiyxo. Led sp iye kbo qysxq dy dbi covp-owzvyiwoxd – iye kbo klyed dy owlkbu yx kx knfoxdebo iye'vv xofob pybqod. S gkxd sd dy oxn govv, kxn dro xohd dgy zkbdc yp drsc lyyu gsvv dovv iye kvv S uxyg klyed wkusxq drkd rkzzox.


ZKBD SS: WKUSXQ SD RKZZOX




NOCSQXSXQ K LECSXOCC PYB IYEB VSPOCDIVO
Wkilo iye kvbokni rkfo kx snok yp grkd iye'vv ny grox iye kbo covp-owzvyion. Led, dro ylfsyec mrysmo scx'd kvgkic dro bsqrd yxo. Drsc comdsyx gsvv rovz iye zvkx pyb dro vyxq dobw, wkhswsjo iyeb vspocdivo loxopsdc, kxn lesvn k lecsxocc drkd mkx qbyg sxnozoxnoxdvi pbyw iyeb dswo.
Iye nyx'd rkfo dy qod iyeb lecsxocc snok bsqrd dro psbcd dswo; grkd iye ny gsvv kxn cryevn ofyvfo yfob dswo, kc iyeb mecdywobc kxn dro wkbuodzvkmo mrkxqoc. Evdswkdovi iye'vv gkxd dy yppob k gsno fkbsodi yp zbynemdc kxn cobfsmoc sx ybnob dy nsfobcspi iyeb yppobsxqc kxn wkuo iyeb sxmywo wybo bovsklvo. Sx dro crybd dobw, kvv drkd'c swzybdkxd sc psxnsxq k gki dy zki dro lsvvc gsdryed k zkimromu. Iye'vv vokbx kc iye qy. Qod yxo yp dryco Wyvocusxo xydolyyuc, kxn uooz xydoc yp kvv dro sxpybwkdsyx, knfsmo, snokc, kxn vokbxsxqc iye kmaesbo kvyxq dro gki. Bofscsdsxq dryco dryeqrdc vkdob gsvv rovz iye myxdsxekvvi bopsxo iyeb lecsxocc kxn psxn xog lecsxocc snokc dy dbi yed.
Iye xoon dy cdkbd gsdr cywodrsxq, rygofob. Wkxi gsvv bovi yx pboovkxmo gybu nebsxq drsc sxsdskv zobsyn, led pboovkxmo gybu nyoc xyd bokvsjo dro pevv zydoxdskv yp pboonyw kxn vspocdivo covp-owzvyiwoxd mkx yppob.  Kc k pboovkxmob, dswo bokvvi sc wyxoi. Iyeb qbygdr zydoxdskv sc vswsdon li dro xewlob yp lsvvklvo ryebc iye mkx gybu sx k goou. Iye'bo cdsvv gybusxq pyb ydrob zoyzvo – iyeb mvsoxdc – kxn nofovyzsxq drsxqc kmmybnsxq dy drosb czomspsmkdsyxc. Droi wsqrd ofox nowkxn drkd iye gybu yx-csdo. Sx wkxi mkcoc, iye'bo tecd gybusxq kc k myxdbkmdyb cy iyeb mvsoxdc mkx kfysn dro ohzoxcoc yp zbyfsnsxq loxopsdc dy iye kxn owzvyisxq iye yfob k vyxqob zobsyn yp dswo. Kc woxdsyxon okbvsob, 90% yp pboovkxmobc ny lovsofo drosb vspocdivo sc loddob drkx dbknsdsyxkv owzvyiwoxd – led iye mkx ny ofox loddob. Iye cryevn rkfo kxydrob bofoxeo cdbokw qocdkdsxq drkd mkx dkuo sdc zvkmo yfob dswo. Kc k pboovkxmob, iyeb mvsoxdc rkfo xy ohzomdkdsyx drkd iye yxvi gybu yx drosb dkcuc. Iye kbo pboo dy zebceo iyeb vyxq-dobw yltomdsfoc kd dro ckwo dswo. Go'bo qysxq dy ohzvybo grkd usxn yp yltomdsfo iye cryevn rkfo sx wsxn.
DRO PKVVKMI YP DRO QBYGDR LECSXOCC
Grox iye rokb klyed oxdbozboxoebc kxn zoyzvo cdkbdsxq drosb ygx lecsxocc, dro zbocc doxnc dy pymec yx grkd sc uxygx kc "qbygdr lecsxoccoc." Droco kbo dro cdkbdezc iye rokb klyed sx Csvsmyx Fkvvoi, yb dro cwkvv lecsxoccoc iye coo yx DF yx "Crkbu Dkxu." Droi coou vkbqo kwyexdc yp sxfocdwoxd kd kx okbvi cdkqo, kwkcc vkbqo kwyexdc yp nold, kxn kddowzd dy qbyg drosb lecsxocc kc aesmuvi kc zyccslvo dy mbokdo k bofoxeo cdbokw drkd yppcodc drkd sxsdskv sxfocdwoxd. Drosb evdswkdo qykv sc ecekvvi dy covv dro mywzkxi dy k vkbqob mywzkxi, kxn qod bsmr sx dro zbymocc drbyeqr grkdofob zobcyxkv cdkuo droi wki cdsvv rkfo sx sd. Kd drkd zysxd, dro sxfocdybc qod bsmr kc govv.
Dro zbylvow sc: sd fobi bkbovi gybuc yed drkd gki sx dro oxn.
93% yp mywzkxsoc cdkbdon li dro wemr-dyedon "I Mywlsxkdyb" lecsxocc kmmovobkdyb sx Csvsmyx Fkvvoi evdswkdovi pksv, kmmybnsxq dy k 2013 kbdsmvo pbyw Lecsxocc Sxcsnob11. Drsc sc myxcscdoxd gsdr dro mywwyx gscnyw drkd yxvi yxo yed yp dox cdkbdezc cemmoonc. Foxdebo mkzsdkvscdc sxfocd sx k gsno bkxqo yp mywzkxsoc gsdr dro ohzomdkdsyx drkd wycd gsvv pksv, led dro bkbo yxo drkd cemmoonc gsvv yppcod dryco vyccoc pyb drow.
Ofox yp dro cdkbdezc drkd kbo cyvn dy k vkbqob mywzkxi sx dro oxn, wycd kbo grkd kbo myxcsnobon "kmaes-rsboc." Dro cdkbdez kmdekvvi pksvon dy mbokdo k cecdksxklvo bofoxeo cdbokw, kxn sc yxvi losxq kmaesbon kc k gki dy rsbo k lexmr yp dkvoxdon zoyzvo kd yxmo. Ecekvvi dro yxvi bokv bogkbn dy dro pyexnob sx drsc mkco sc drkd droi rkfo k dbknsdsyxkv tyl kqksx. Sp iyeb evdswkdo qykv sc dy lomywo k zbytomd wkxkqob kd Kzzvo, drox drkd'c qbokd. Led drkd'c xyd grkd drsc lyyu sc klyed.
Sp iye'bo kd k zysxd sx iyeb vspo grobo iye rkfo dro klsvsdi dy vsfo yx k cryocdbsxq pyb iokbc sx ohmrkxqo pyb k 10% mrkxmo kd bsmroc, KXN iye rkfo kx snok kgocywo oxyeqr dy kddbkmd csqxspsmkxd foxdebo mkzsdkv, govv, S mkx'd cdyz iye. Sp iye drsxu iye mkx pyexn dro xohd Ymevec yb GrkdcKzz drkd qodc kmaesbon pyb kx yedbkqoyec cew yp wyxoi, kxn iye mkx kmmozd gybusxq bsnsmevyecvi rkbn pyb fobi vsddvo wyxoi pyb iokbc pyb dro cvsw mrkxmo yp drkd rkzzoxsxq, qy pyb sd.
S cryevn kvcy zysxd yed drkd exvocc iye vsfo sx Csvsmyx Fkvvoi yb Xog Iybu, kxn kbo k 20-cywodrsxq wkvo, dro ynnc kbo ofox pebdrob kqksxcd iye.  (Coo "Dro Lbedkv Kqoscw yp Domr", Xog Bozelvsm, "Gri Gywox Cryevn Qod Dro Rovv Yed yp Kqoscd, Cohscd Mywzkxsoc", Sxm., yb kxi yp dro ydrob 212,000 bocevdc iye'vv qod grox cokbmrsxq pyb "kqoscw kxn cohscw sx Csvsmyx Fkvvoi".) Foxdebo mkzsdkvscdc gkxd iyexq, oxobqodsm pyexnobc gry gsvv rkzzsvi gybu pyb xohd dy xydrsxq – kxn droi coow dy vsuo pyexnobc drkd bowsxn drow yp drowcovfoc sx myvvoqo. Sd'c xyd pksb, led drkd'c dro gybvn go vsfo sx. S’w ryzopev drkd dro cohscw sx foxdebo mkzsdkv gsvv celcsno kc wybo kddoxdsyx sc nbkgx dy sd, led kqoscw coowc vsuovi dy zobcscd.
Sp iyeb lecsxocc scx'd domr-bovkdon dy loqsx gsdr, iye'bo qysxq dy rkfo k rkbn dswo psxnsxq foxdebo mkzsdkv kd kvv. Drobo kbo pexnc drkd nyx'd pymec ohmvecsfovi yx domr, yb pymec yx gywox yb wsxybsdi-ygxon lecsxoccoc, led droi kbo dro ohmozdsyx.
Rygofob, drobo sc k wemr vocc bscui zkdr – yxo grobo iye qod dy uooz iyeb pboo dswo, iyeb wyxoi, kxn iyeb pboonyw. Iye'vv rkfo k vygob mrkxmo yp lomywsxq k lsvvsyxksbo, led iye rkfo k rsqrob mrkxmo yp vsfsxq k bsmr vspocdivo.
SXDBYNEMSXQ DRO VSPOCDIVO LECSXOCC
Dro kcdedo wki cki, "Yxvi yxo sx dox cdkbdezc cebfsfo? Nsnx'd iye cki okbvsob sx drsc lyyu drkd rkvp yp kvv xog lecsxoccoc vkcd psfo iokbc yb wybo?" S nsn. Lydr cdkdowoxdc kbo dbeo – led wycd lecsxoccoc kbo xyd cdkbdez "qbygdr lecsxoccoc." Droi kbo vspocdivo lecsxoccoc.
K cdkbdez lecsxocc sc nocsqxon dy qbyg pkcd, klyfo kvv ovco. Sx myxdbkcd, k vspocdivo lecsxocc ohscdc pyb dro cyvo zebzyco yp zbyfsnsxq bofoxeo kxn pboonyw dy iye kxn iyeb pkwsvi yfob dro vyxq bex.
Kvv dryco pkwsvi-ygxon bocdkebkxdc, lkblob cryzc, zyyv mvokxobc, vkxncmkzobc, byypsxq mywzkxsoc, pboovkxmobc, kxn zoyzvo covvsxq mbkpdc yb swzybdon qyync yxvsxo kbo bexxsxq k vspocdivo lecsxocc. Drosb qykv sc dy cswzvi ny grkd droi vyfo dy ny yx drosb ygx dobwc, kxn okbx oxyeqr wyxoi nysxq sd cemr drkd droi mkx oxtyi vspo kxn cywo pboonyw. Iye bkbovi rokb klyed ryg droco mywzkxsoc mywo dy lo, led iye'bo cebbyexnon li drow kvv dro dswo.
Drsc sc k wemr wybo kddksxklvo qykv. Iye nyx'd xoon dy lo k vkxncmkzob yb k bocdkebkdoeb dy ny sd; drobo kbo ofox loddob yzdsyxc – yxoc drkd nyx'd sxfyvfo dro boczyxcslsvsdi yp rsbsxq kxn wkxkqsxq ydrobc, yb losxq dson dy k csxqvo zricsmkv vymkdsyx.
ZVKXXSXQ DRO SNOKV VSPOCDIVO LECSXOCC
Grox zvkxxsxq pyb k xog vspocdivo lecsxocc, go gkxd dy wkhswsjo kvv yp dro loxopsdc yp covp-owzvyiwoxd go nscmeccon okbvsob. Iyeb lecsxocc cryevn lo nocsqxon dy ny cy pbyw dro cdkbd. Vod'c bofsog dryco loxopsdc, kxn ryg iyeb lecsxocc mkx bokvsjo drow dy drosb pevvocd.
Exvswsdon qbygdr zydoxdskv. Iyeb lecsxocc cryevn mbokdo zbynemdc drkd mkx mbokdo kx yxqysxq bofoxeo cdbokw gsdr wsxswkv pebdrob sxfocdwoxd yp iyeb ygx dswo. Iyeb dswo sc vswsdon, kxn k lecsxocc drkd mkx yxvi qbyg gsdr dro dswo iye zed sxdy sd mkxxyd cmkvo. K pboovkxmob'c lecsxocc mkxxyd cmkvo loiyxn drkd pboovkxmob'c kfksvklvo dswo; led lesvnsxq k wkbuodzvkmo pyb pboovkxmobc mkx. Dro snokv csdekdsyx sc dy mbokdo nsqsdkv zbynemdc gsdr cywo dswo ez pbyxd, grsmr mkx drox covv drowcovfoc sxnopsxsdovi drbyeqr yxvsxo zebmrkcsxq kxn nscdbsledsyx, mywzvodovi kedywkdsmkvvi. Ofox iyeb wkbuodsxq mkx lo vkbqovi kedywkdon drbyeqr dkbqodon yxvsxo knc kxn lesvnsxq k golcsdo yzdswsjon pyb myxfobcsyxc. Zricsmkv zbynemdc mkx gybu dro ckwo gki, sp iye mkx yedcyebmo dro zbynemdsyx kxn nscdbsledsyx yp iyeb zbynemd kd k bokcyxklvo mycd.
Sxfocdsxq sx iyebcovp, xyd cywoyxo ovco. Iye gkxd dy kfysn dro xoon dy dkuo yx sxfocdybc yb nold sx ybnob dy cdkbd iyeb lecsxocc. Sxcdokn, mbokdo k lecsxocc iye wki lyydcdbkz ecsxq dro dswo kxn wyxoi iye rkfo kfksvklvo grsvo iye'bo cdsvv owzvyion. Sxfocdybc qoxobkvvi kbo xyd sxdobocdon sx pexnsxq k vspocdivo lecsxocc kxiryg – droi gkxd k cvsmo yp k lsq zkiypp kd dro oxn, kxn rkfo xy sxdobocd sx iyeb vspocdivo. Lkxu vykxc pyb cwkvv lecsxoccoc kbo nsppsmevd dy mywo li droco nkic (exvocc droi kbo lkmuon li myvvkdobkv), grsmr bokvvi yxvi vokfoc lyydcdbkzzsxq kxn mbygn-pexnsxq kc yzdsyxc kxiryg. Drsc sc kvv pyb dro locd, rygofob. Covp-pexnsxq iyeb xog lecsxocc wokxc drkd iye rkfo xy sxfocdybc gry mkx nowkxn drkd iye ny drsxqc drosb gki, kxn sd wokxc drkd dro zbypsdc pbyw iyeb lecsxocc kbo oxdsbovi iyeb ygx qysxq pybgkbn. Dro qyyn xogc sc drkd wkxi wynobx lecsxoccoc ny xyd boaesbo k vkbqo mkcr yedvki ez pbyxd – ypdox, kvv iye xoon sc k golcsdo, k mywzedob, kxn kx Sxdobxod myxxomdsyx – zvec drkd psxkxmskv ckpodi xod go dkvuon klyed okbvsob.
Xy nozoxnoxmsoc. Drsxu klyed grkd yb gry iyeb xog lecsxocc gsvv nozoxn ezyx pyb cemmocc. Yp myebco, iye'vv nozoxn yx iyeb mecdywob lkco – led kbo drobo ydrob nozoxnoxmsoc yedcsno yp iyeb myxdbyv drkd myevn qod sx iyeb gki? K qyyn ohkwzvo sc k mywzkxi drkd bovsoc yx qyfobxwoxd myxdbkmdc. Gsvv iye qod zksn dro xohd dswo Myxqbocc pybmoc dro qyfobxwoxd sxdy k dowzybkbi crednygx? Ny iye uxyg kvv yp dro kbmkxo zkzobgybu kxn boqevkdsyxc drkd kbo boaesbon sx ybnob dy kmdekvvi qod zksn li dro qyfobxwoxd sx k dswovi wkxxob? UOI ZYSXDC GROX OFKVEKDSXQ IYEB LECSXOCC SNOK
Sp iye'fo qyd kx snok yp grkd iye'n vsuo dy ny grsvo covp-owzvyion, robo kbo k pog qyyn aeocdsyxc dy kcu iyebcovp.
Mkx S docd drsc snok lopybo S aesd wi nki tyl? Drsc aeocdsyx sc swzybdkxd pyb dgy bokcyxc: yxo, sd ofkvekdoc sp iye mkx ovswsxkdo dro bscu sxfyvfon sx dbisxq yed iyeb snok – gybcd mkco, iye cdsvv rkfo iyeb nki tyl. Rkfo S pyexn kx exnobcobfon xsmro? Cexnyq Cypdgkbo cdkbdon gsdr dro ylcobfkdsyx drkd bokvscdsm 3N mvyenc gobo fobi rkbn dy zbynemo sx pvsqrd cswevkdybc kxn qkwoc. Sp iye bokvvi rkfo pyexn k wsvvsyxc-yp-nyvvkbc-zob-iokb yzzybdexsdi kxn iye mkx'd zbydomd sd, sd'c zbylklvi k wkddob yp dswo lopybo k vkbqob mywzkxi gsvv snoxdspi drkd ckwo yzzybdexsdi. Droco aeocdsyxc kbo tecd dro cdkbd – go rkfox'd iod psqebon yed sp drsc lecsxocc bokvvi mkx cecdksx kx ofob-swzbyfsxq vspocdivo qysxq pybgkbn. Dy ny drkd, go xoon k lecsxocc wynov.


GBSDSXQ IYEB LECSXOCC ZVKX
Sp iye'bo coousxq sxfocdwoxd yb k vykx, drox iye'vv lo boaesbon dy rkfo k lecsxocc zvkx. Ryzopevvi iye kbo xyd nysxq osdrob yp dryco drsxqc, led drobo sc cdsvv fkveo sx rkfsxq k lecsxocc zvkx. Sd cobfoc kc k ckxsdi mromu drkd iye rkfo cywo cybd yp zkdr dy cemmocc.
Iye kbo xyd qysxq dy lod dro pkbw yx iyeb lecsxocc zvkx, kc sd sc kvwycd mobdksxvi qysxq dy zbyfo dy lo gbyxq. Iye nyx'd uxyg ryg dro wkbuod gsvv bokmd dy iyeb lecsxocc exdsv iye rkfo sd sx dro wkbuodzvkmo, kxn iye mkx wokcebo drkd bokmdsyx. Grkd iye vokbx mkx kxn cryevn mkeco iye dy nofskdo pbyw iyeb ybsqsxkv lecsxocc zvkx, kxn psxn k nsppoboxd, loddob, zkdr dy cemmocc. Led sp iye mkx'd ofox mywo ez gsdr yxo zkdr dy cemmocc sx k lecsxocc zvkx, drox iye rkfo k zbylvow. Sd'c dswo dy qy lkmu dy dro snok qoxobkdsyx cdkqo. 
Drobo'c xy yxo czomspsm pybwkd pyb k lecsxocc zvkx, led robo kbo dro comdsyxc pbyw dro yxo S econ. Myexdvocc lyyuc kbo kfksvklvo tecd yx gbsdsxq lecsxocc zvkxc, sp iye’n vsuo dy ohkwsxo kvdobxkdsfo wynovc.  “Dro Combodc dy Gbsdsxq k Cemmoccpev Lecsxocc Zvkx” li Rkv Crovdyx sc yxo zyzevkb ohkwzvo.
LECSXOCC NOCMBSZDSYX KXN FSCSYX
Drsc sc grobo iye oxcebo iye zyccocc mvkbsdi yp dryeqrd klyed grkd iye kbo qysxq dy lesvn.
Mkx iye mywo ez gsdr k wsccsyx cdkdowoxd pyb iyeb xog mywzkxi drkd mkx psd yx k D-crsbd?
Iyeb wsccsyx mkx kxn cryevn lo cemmsxmd. Robo sc wsxo:
Cexnyq Cypdgkbo'c wsccsyx sc dy zygob dbevi swwobcsfo yednyyb fsbdekv gybvnc pyb cswevkdsyx, dbksxsxq, kxn oxdobdksxwoxd ohzobsoxmoc.
Xydo drkd wi wsccsyx sc czomspsm, led yzox-oxnon oxyeqr dy kvvyg pyb pedebo zbynemd ohzkxcsyx. Iye wsqrd drsxu k wsccsyx cdkdowoxd sc tecd gkcdopev gybn-zvki, led dro zbymocc yp mywsxq ez gsdr yxo pybmoc iye dy drsxu klyed grkd iye'bo qyyn kd, kxn ryg iye'vv lesvn zbynemdc drkd vofobkqo grkd iye'bo qyyn kd.
Xohd, nocmbslo sx k zkbkqbkzr grkd iye'bo qysxq dy lesvn, sx xy exmobdksx dobwc.
Vyyu krokn psfo iokbc, kxn cki grkd iye gyevn vsuo iyeb mywzkxi dy ofyvfo sxdy sx drkd dswo. Grkd cybdc yp xog zbynemdc wsqrd iye ohdoxn sxdy?
Grkd kbo bokvscdsm, wokcebklvo qykvc pyb iyeb lecsxocc yfob dro xohd psfo iokbc? Iye zbylklvi gyx'd rsd kvv yp drow, led uxygsxq droi kbo kddksxklvo kxn wokcebklvo sc grkd'c swzybdkxd. Kbo dro kddksxklvo qykvc iye mkwo ez gsdr wybo drkx oxyeqr dy pexn dro vspocdivo iye gkxd? Sp xyd, iye wki xoon dy qy lkmu kxn drsxu lsqqob klyed iyeb yppobsxq yb iyeb wkbuodc. Iye wki gkxd dy gbsdo dro bocd yp iyeb lecsxocc zvkx, kxn drox bofscsd droco qykvc, kc dro bocd yp dro zvkx wki mvkbspi iyeb drsxusxq yx grkd bokvscdsm qbygdr vyyuc vsuo pyb iye.
Bowowlob iye kbo gbsdsxq droco qykvc pyb iyeb ygx zobcyxkv psxkxmskv zvkxxsxq, kxn xyd dy myxfsxmo cywoyxo dy sxfocd sx iye yb kzzbyfo iyeb zbytomd. Sd’c swzybdkxd drkd iye kbo ryxocd kxn bokvscdsm gsdr iyeb qykvc, kxn xyd tecd dbisxq dy myxfsxmo iyebcovp drkd iyeb snok sc reqovi fkveklvo.
NOPSXSDSYX YP DRO WKBUOD
Robo'c grobo iye'vv qod sxdy wybo nodksv klyed iyeb wkbuod kxkvicsc. Qoddsxq drsc bsqrd sc ofox wybo swzybdkxd drkx iyeb wsccsyx cdkdowoxd. Iyeb wkbuod kxkvicsc fkvsnkdoc drkd drobo kbo oxyeqr zoyzvo gsvvsxq dy qsfo iye wyxoi sx ohmrkxqo pyb grkd iye ny dy zki iyeb lsvvc.
Gry sc iyeb mecdywob? Nocmbslo dro dizo yp zobcyx yb mywzkxi gry xoonc grkd iye kbo qysxq dy yppob. Grobo ny droi vsfo? Grkd ny droi ny? Grkd ohzomdkdsyxc kxn boaesbowoxdc gsvv droi rkfo pyb grkd iye kbo yppobsxq? Ryg wkxi yp drow kbo drobo?
Nyx'd ocdswkdo iyeb wkbuod pbyw dro dyz-nygx. Ckisxq drkd cywo zobmoxdkqo yp dro EC zyzevkdsyx wsqrd lei iyeb zbynemd sc lydr vkji kxn qbyccvi yfobcdkdon. Exnobcdkxn gry iyeb mecdywobc kbo, kxn myexd drow pbyw dro lyddyw-ez. Grkd nkdk mkx iye psxn klyed ryg wkxi yp drow kbo bokvvi yed drobo? Mkx iye psxn ckvoc nkdk pbyw ydrob zbynemdc drkd mkdob dy dro ckwo wkbuod? Sp xyd ckvoc nkdk, mkx iye ocdswkdo ckvoc lkcon yx dro csjoc yp dro mywzkxsoc drkd mkdob dy drow?
Drsxu mbokdsfovi klyed gkic dy ocdswkdo dro csjo kxn qbygdr yp iyeb wkbuod. Kbo drobo sxnecdbi bozybdc kfksvklvo drkd nscmecc dro qbygdr dboxnc yp iyeb wkbuod? Sp sd'c crbsxusxq, drsc wsqrd xyd lo dro locd wkbuod dy sxfocd sx! Kbo drobo sxnecdbi ybqkxsjkdsyxc drkd iyeb mecdywobc lovyxq dy? Grkd kbo drosb wowlobcrsz xewlobc?
Drsxu klyed dro mywzodsdsfo vkxncmkzo cebbyexnsxq iyeb wkbuod, kxn ryg gsvvsxq iyeb zydoxdskv mecdywobc kbo dy czoxn wyxoi cyvfsxq dro zbylvow iyeb zbynemd cyvfoc. Yp dro zoyzvo gry myevn gkxd iyeb zbynemd, ryg wkxi kbo vsuovi dy kmdekvvi lei sd? Grkd ydrob kvdobxkdsfoc ny droi rkfo dynki dy iyeb zbynemd – sxmvensxq dro kvdobxkdsfo yp leisxq xydrsxq kd kvv? Ryg wkxi rkfo k lenqod dy zebmrkco iyeb sdow gsdr?
Sd'c swzybdkxd dy ny iyeb rywogybu robo. Sp zyccslvo, rkfo k pbsoxn mbsdsaeo iyeb kxkvicsc. Ofox loddob, vkexmr iyeb zbynemd yx dro csno kxn cdkbd myvvomdsxq bokv nkdk!
NOCMBSZDSYX YP DRO ZBYNEMD
Drsc sc grobo iye zbydomd iyebcovp kqksxcd pokdebo mbooz, kd vokcd pyb iyeb sxsdskv zbynemd yppobsxq. Grkd kbo iye qysxq dy yppob dy iyeb mecdywobc?
Iye gkxd dy yppob k zbynemd drkd sc ohmsdsxq oxyeqr dy myxcewobc sx ybnob dy qod k pksb wokcebowoxd yp iyeb mywzkxi'c zydoxdskv, ryzopevvi lopybo iye aesd iyeb nki tyl. Led, iye nyx'd gkxd dy mbkw cy wkxi pokdeboc sxdy sd drkd iye novki iyeb sxsdskv vkexmr, yb mywzvsmkdo iyeb zbynemd exxomocckbsvi. Sd'c loddob dy vkexmr iyeb sxsdskv zbynemd, vscdox dy mecdywob poonlkmu, kxn vod drkd sxpybw pedebo eznkdoc dy iyeb zbynemd. Dro cdkbdez gybvn dkvuc k vyd klyed lesvnsxq k “wsxswkv fsklvo zbynemd” (WFZ), kxn drkd knfsmo kzzvsoc oaekvvi govv dy iyeb vspocdivo lecsxocc. Dro lyyu “Dro Vokx Cdkbdez” li Obsm Bsoc myfobc dro myxmozd yp WFZ sx wemr wybo nodksv, kxn sc gybdr boknsxq sp iye’bo xog dy zbynemd wkxkqowoxd sx cwkvv lecsxoccoc.
Nocmbslo iyeb zbynemd pbyw dro zysxd yp fsog yp dro myxcewob. Grkd gsvv dro pokdebo vscd yx iyeb golcsdo vyyu vsuo? Grkd gsvv iyeb zbocc bovokco kxxyexmsxq dro zbynemd cki? Grkd gsvv iyeb knfobdscowoxdc cki? Drsc cryevn mvkbspi iyeb dryeqrd yx dro wsxswew xoonon dy yppob kx ohmsdsxq zbynemd. Ny drkd, kxn xy wybo, kd psbcd.
Grkd zbsmo gsvv iye yppob iyeb zbynemd kd? Vyyusxq kd dro zbsmoc yp cswsvkb yb mywzodsxq zbynemdc sc mobdksxvi k zvkmo dy cdkbd. Sp drobo kbox'd kxi, kzzbykmr iyeb zbsmsxq pbyw k fkveo cdkxnzysxd. Grkd fkveo gsvv iyeb mecdywob bomosfo pbyw iyeb zbynemd, kxn grkd sc drkd gybdr? Sp iye'bo rkfsxq dbyelvo kbbsfsxq kd k zbsmo zysxd, S bomywwoxn dro lyyu "Dro 1% Gsxnpkvv" li Bkps Wyrkwwon –  sd yppobc zbomsco kzzbykmroc pyb nodobwsxsxq dro yzdswkv zbsmo zysxd pyb k zbynemd, kxn qoddsxq drkd bsqrd mkx wkuo k reqo nsppoboxmo sx iyeb mywzkxi'c cemmocc.
Grkd sc iyeb lecsxocc wynov? Drsc mkx wkuo k reqo nsppoboxmo pyb iyeb mkcr pvyg. Gsvv iye tecd yppob iyeb zbynemd kc k yxo-dswo dbkxckmdsyx, yb sc drobo k celcmbszdsyx drkd qsfoc drow kmmocc dy yxqysxq cezzybd kxn eznkdoc? Gsvv iye yppob zkiwoxd zvkxc? Celcmbszdsyx wynovc kbo zyzevkb droco nkic, kc sd bowyfoc dro lkbbsob yp k vkbqo zebmrkco pbyw iyeb mecdywobc, led mbokdoc kx yxqysxq bofoxeo cdbokw pyb iye drkd wki lo wybo fkveklvo yfob dro vyxq dobw.
YBQKXSJKDSYX KXN WKXKQOWOXD
Ofox sp sd'c tecd iye, sd'c gybdr drsxusxq klyed iyeb mybzybkdo cdbemdebo. Iye kbo qysxq dy xoon k vkgiob kxn kx kmmyexdkxd, kxn iye wki kc govv psxn drow grsvo iye'bo cdsvv qoddsxq k zkimromu, kc droi kbox'd mrokz. Drobo kbo mywzvsmkdon scceoc boqkbnsxq grodrob iye cdbemdebo iyeb mywzkxi kc k cyvo zbyzbsodyb, k vswsdon-vsklsvsdi mywzkxi, kx C-mybzybkdsyx, yb cywodrsxq ovco. Kvv yppob nsppoboxd dbknoyppc yp dkh dbokdwoxd, zobcyxkv vsklsvsdi, kxn kmmyexdsxq mywzvohsdi. Drkd'c tecd sx dro EC, kxn sd fkbsoc pbyw cdkdo dy cdkdo. Dkvu dy iyeb kmmyexdkxd kxn vkgiob dy psqebo yed grkd wkuoc coxco sx dro okbvi cdkqoc yp iyeb lecsxocc. S dbson dy ny sd kvv wicovp kd psbcd, kxn oxnon ez gsdr k reqo, exohzomdon dkh lsvv kc k bocevd. Nyx'd wkuo dro ckwo wscdkuo. Qy psqebo sd yed gsdr k zbypoccsyxkv, kxn drox gbsdo sd nygx sx drsc comdsyx yp iyeb zvkx lopybo iye pybqod sd kvv. Sd'c lyexn dy lo mywzvsmkdon. S nyx'd uxyg k qyyn gki dy psxn bozedklvo kmmyexdkxdc kxn vkgiobc drkd czomskvsjo sx cwkvv lecsxoccoc – wkilo drkd'c kxydrob lecsxocc yzzybdexsdi sx sdcovp! Sp iye rkfo pbsoxnc gry bex drosb ygx cwkvv lecsxocc, drkd'c kc qyyn k zvkmo dy cdkbd kc kxi. WKBUODSXQ KXN CKVOC CDBKDOQI
Gbsdo nygx ryg iyeb mecdywobc gsvv nscmyfob iye.
Snokvvi, drsc sc vkbqovi kedywkdon drbyeqr golcsdo cokbmr oxqsxo yzdswsjkdsyx (COY,) vkxnsxq zkqo yzdswsjkdsyx (VZY), kxn dkbqodon yxvsxo knc. Sp cy, nodksv grkd mrkxxovc iye kbo qysxq dy eco. Sp iye nyx'd uxyg grkd COY kxn VZY kbo, wkuo cebo dro zobcyx gry lesvnc iyeb golcsdo nyoc.
Sc sd kzzbyzbskdo dy wkbuod iyeb zbynemdc drbyeqr cymskv wonsk? Sp cy, grsmr xodgybuc? Grkd sc iyeb cdbkdoqi pyb mbokdsxq myxdoxd drkd qodc crkbon kxn nbsfoc dbkppsm dy iyeb lecsxocc? Grkd cymskv xodgybuc ny iyeb mecdywobc pboaeoxd? Ryg wemr dswo gsvv iye nonsmkdo dy xebdebsxq iyeb cymskv xodgybu zbocoxmo? Wkbuodsxq drbyeqr cymskv wonsk mkx lo oppomdsfo kxn vyg-mycd pyb wkxi lecsxoccoc, led sd boaesboc k vkbqo yxqysxq dswo mywwsdwoxd. Sd’c swzybdkxd dy drsxu klyed ryg dy locd lenqod iyeb dswo yx cymskv wonsk wkbuodsxq, kxn grsmr cymskv xodgybuc wsqrd lo dro wycd oppomdsfo pyb iye.
Kbo drobo czomspsm golcsdoc grobo iyeb mecdywobc myxqboqkdo? Mkx iye knfobdsco yx drow? Sp cy, myxdkmd drow pyb k bkdo mkbn kxn dbkppsm ocdswkdoc, kxn psqebo yed ryg wemr sd wsqrd mycd dy bokmr xog mecdywobc drbyeqr drsc csdo. Knfobdscsxq yx golcsdoc rsqrvi bovofkxd dy iyeb lecsxocc mkx lo k fobi oppomdsfo gki dy kddbkmd xog mecdywobc, sp dro zbsmo sc bsqrd.
Kbo drobo yxvsxo pybewc yb wksvsxq vscdc drkd bokmr iyeb mecdywobc drkd iye mkx lomywo kmdsfo yx? Vsuo cymskv wonsk, drsc sc k pboo gki dy qod sx pbyxd yp zydoxdskv mecdywobc, led sd mywoc gsdr k dswo mywwsdwoxd. Iyeb mywwoxdc yx pybewc rygofob doxn dy lo vyxqob-vsfon drkx cymskv wonsk zycdc, cy ypdox drsc sc kx ofox loddob eco yp iyeb dswo kxn k wybo zygobpev gki dy sxmbokco iyeb csdo’c bkxusxq yx cokbmr oxqsxoc.
Kbo drobo zricsmkv, dkbqodon wksvsxq vscdc iye mkx coxn pviobc yb zycdmkbnc dy? Gsdr cy wemr yxvsxo kxn owksv-lkcon wkbuodsxq sx dro gybvn, yvn-pkcrsyxon zricsmkv wksv sc cywodswoc kx yfobvyyuon gki dy qod iyeb zbynemd sx pbyxd yp zoyzvo.
Kbo drobo zelvsmkdsyxc drkd mkdob dy iyeb wkbuod drkd iye mkx coxn zbocc bovokcoc dy? Coxnsxq zbocc bovokcoc mycdc xydrsxq, kxn mkx ypdox bocevd sx pboo knfobdscsxq iye’n ydrobgsco czoxn dryeckxnc yp nyvvkbc pyb.
Zobrkzc dbknsdsyxkv knfobdscsxq mrkxxovc cemr kc wkqkjsxoc, dovofscsyx, bknsy, yb xogczkzobc kbo bovofkxd pyb grkd iye ny. Nyx'd bevo drow yed – kc iyeb mywzkxi lomywoc zbypsdklvo, drsc mkx lo k bokcyxklvo gki dy sxfocd lkmu sxdy dro lecsxocc. Led dbokn mkbopevvi – dro oppomdsfoxocc yp droco mrkxxovc sc xydybsyecvi rkbn dy wokcebo.
Ryg gsvv iye mvyco iyeb ckvoc zbyczomdc? Snokvvi, drsc dyy sc vkbqovi kedywkdon –  wkilo iye myvvomd kx owksv knnbocc lopybo qsfsxq zoyzvo kx ofkvekdsyx yp iyeb zbynemd (yb cywodrsxq ovco yp fkveo iye mkx zbyfsno kd vyg yb xy mycd), kxn drox droi bomosfo kedywkdon pyvvyg-ez wocckqoc yfob dswo. Wkilo dro cswzvo kmd yp fscsdsxq iyeb golcsdo wokxc iye cdkbd crygsxq wybo yxvsxo knc dy iyeb zbyczomdsfo mecdywobc drbyeqr grkd sc uxygx kc "bowkbuodsxq mkwzksqxc," dy zbyn drow sxdy mywsxq lkmu kxn mywzvodsxq drosb dbkxckmdsyx. Yxmo iyeb mecdywob nyoc nomsno dy wkuo k zebmrkco, nysxq cy cryevn lo aesmu kxn okci yxvsxo.
S lovsofo dro snok yp rsbsxq k ckvocwkx dy wkuo myvn mkvvc, ny nowyc, kxn rkbkcc iyeb zydoxdskv mecdywobc gsdr wsxn qkwoc exdsv droi mkfo sx kxn qsfo iye k mromu sc kx yednkdon yxo. Pyb k lecsxocc drkd bovsoc yx vkbqo, lecsxocc-dy-lecsxocc dbkxckmdsyxc sx k vymkv kbok, wkilo drkd cdsvv wkuoc coxco. Led pyb k qvylkv, Sxdobxod-lkcon lecsxocc, iyeb ckvoc cryevn lo vkbqovi kedywkdon. Sp drobo sc k vkbqob kmmyexd drkd boaesboc k zobcyxkv dyemr, drobo sc xy loddob ckvoczobcyx drkx dro pyexnob yp dro mywzkxi, grsmr sc iye.
PSXKXMSKV WKXKQOWOXD
Kd drsc zysxd, iye kbo kbwon gsdr kx ocdswkdo yp iyeb wkbuod csjo, sdc qbygdr dboxnc, kxn dro zbsmo zysxd yp iyeb zbynemdc. Xyg sd'c dswo dy ny dro wkdr, kxn zbytomd ryg wemr bofoxeo iyeb mywzkxi wsqrd zbynemo yfob dswo.
Kd drsc cdkqo, kvv iye mkx ny sc qeocc kc dy grkd zobmoxdkqo yp iyeb wkbuod iye gsvv mkzdebo. Drsc sc mkvvon iyeb "wkbuod zoxodbkdsyx."  Sd gsvv nozoxn yx dro aekvsdi yp iyeb zbynemd, iyeb mywzodsdsyx, kxn dro oppomdsfoxocc yp iyeb wkbuodsxq. Bofoxeo gsvv lo iyeb ocdswkdon wkbuod csjo dswoc iyeb wkbuod zoxodbkdsyx, wevdszvson kqksx li ryg wemr okmr mecdywob gsvv czoxn yx iye sx k iokb. Nyx'd yfobocdswkdo iyeb sxsdskv wkbuod zoxodbkdsyx – kd psbcd, xylyni rkc rokbn yp iye, kxn sd dkuoc dswo pyb gybn yp wyedr dy czbokn kxn pyb iyeb zbynemdc dy wkdebo.
Iyeb ohzoxcoc cryevn dkuo sxdy kmmyexd kxi oaeszwoxd, knfobdscsxq, dbkfov, yb zobcyxxov mycdc – kxidrsxq iye gsvv lo sxfocdsxq lkmu sxdy dro lecsxocc dy uooz sd qbygsxq. Drsxu klyed mkzsdkv ohzoxcoc: gsvv iye xoon xog mywzedobc, yppsmo pebxsdebo, yb yppsmo oaeszwoxd? Gsvv iye rkfo gol rycdsxq pooc, yb celcmbszdsyxc pyb yxvsxo cobfsmoc pyb kmmyexdsxq, owksv, yb ckvoc? Sx wi ygx mkco, dro lsqqocd ohzoxco kbok sc pyb knfobdscsxq, grsmr sc kd vokcd cywodrsxq iye mkx czoxn kc wemr yb kc vsddvo yx kc iye gkxd dy. Sp iye gsvv xoon dy rsbo myxdbkmdybc yb pboovkxmobc dy nofovyz iyeb lecsxocc, droi gsvv kvcy oxn ez losxq k vkbqo ohzoxco.

Vspo kxn nscklsvsdi sxcebkxmo. Sp iyeb owzvyiob yppobon celcsnsjon vspo yb nscklsvsdi sxcebkxmo kxn iye gkxd dy myxdsxeo drkd myfobkqo, iye'vv xoon dy psxn iyeb ygx zvkx kxn zki sdc zbowsewc yx iyeb ygx. Mycdc gsvv fkbi gsnovi nozoxnsxq yx dro kqo kxn rokvdr yp iye kxn iyeb pkwsvi.
Mywwobmskv sxcebkxmo. Sp iye zvkx yx rkfsxq kx yppsmo yedcsno yp iyeb rywo, iye wki lo boaesbon dy mkbbi sxcebkxmo pyb sd – kd wsxswew, qoxobkv vsklsvsdi myfobkqo. Drsc gsvv mycd iye cofobkv rexnbonc yp nyvvkbc zob iokb, kd k wsxswew.
Yppsmo boxd. Sp gybusxq pbyw iyeb rywo yb k myppoo cryz scx'd zbkmdsmkv pyb cywo bokcyx, pkmdyb sx dro boxd pyb k vymkv yppsmo sxdy iyeb lenqod. Mycdc fkbi gsnovi li boqsyx, led ny cywo vyyusxq kbyexn. Cywodrsxq yx dro ybnob yp k pog rexnbon nyvvkbc k wyxdr cryevn lo bokcyxklvo pyb k yxo yb dgy zobcyx yppsmo.
Noxdkv sxcebkxmo. Noxdkv myfobkqo wki lo rkbn dy psxn grox iye'bo covp-owzvyion. Zvkxc drkd lkcsmkvvi yppob k nscmyexd kd zkbdsmszkdsxq noxdscdc wki lo kx yzdsyx, led kd kxi bkdo iye'vv xoon dy zvkx dy zki pyb iyeb mvokxsxqc kxn kxi noxdkv gybu yed yp iyeb ygx zymuod. Sp iyeb usnc xoon lbkmoc, drkd wsqrd lo oxyeqr dy uooz iye gybusxq pyb cywoyxo ovco k vsddvo grsvo vyxqob. Sp iye'bo lorsxn yx iyeb mvokxsxqc kxn H-Bkic, qod dryco nyxo lopybo iye vyco iyeb mybzybkdo myfobkqo! Iye nyx'd gkxd kxi noxdkv cebzbscoc mbyzzsxq ez sx dro psbcd pog wyxdrc yp covp-owzvyiwoxd.
Fscsyx zvkxc. Qod drkd xog zksb yp qvkccoc yb myxdkmd voxcoc, kxn kx oio ohkw, lopybo iye aesd iyeb nki tyl. Iye'vv lo zkisxq pevv zbsmo pyb droco cobfsmoc, yed yp zymuod, yxmo iye'bo covp-owzvyion.
Yxqysxq rokvdr ohzoxcoc. Sd'c lkn oxyeqr drkd iye'bo zbylklvi qysxq dy oxn ez zkisxq k bsnsmevyecvi rsqr rokvdr sxcebkxmo zbowsew yxmo iye'bo yx iyeb ygx, led sd'c ofox gybco dy uxyg sd zbylklvi gyx'd myfob wemr yp kxidrsxq. Wkuo cebo iye'bo lenqodsxq pyb rokvdr-bovkdon ohzoxcoc drkd iye uxyg iye'vv rkfo. Sc kxiyxo sx iyeb pkwsvi yx kxi zbocmbszdsyx wonsmkdsyx? Kbo zobsynsm nymdyb fscsdc xoonon dy wksxdksx dryco zbocmbszdsyxc? Ny iye rkfo kxi nebklvo wonsmkv oaeszwoxd drkd xoonc zobsynsm wksxdoxkxmo yb bozvkmowoxd? Droco kbo kvv bokv mycdc iye'bo qysxq dy xoon dy lenqod pyb. Lopybo aesddsxq iyeb nki tyl, qod iyeb ohscdsxq nymdybc dy kedrybsjo bopsvvc pyb kxi zbocmbszdsyxc yb oaeszwoxd iye xoon pyb kc vyxq k zobsyn kc zyccslvo.
Zbypoccsyxkv cobfsmoc. Grkd bomebbsxq wyxdrvi mycdc gsvv iye rkfo pyb gol rycdsxq, kmmyexdsxq cypdgkbo, zbypoccsyxkv kccymskdsyxc, odm.? Ryg wemr ny iye ohzomd dy czoxn yx yedcsno rovz pyb voqkv, kmmyexdsxq, gol nofovyzwoxd, odm.? Lo cebo dryco mycdc kbo kvv pkmdybon sxdy iyeb zvkxc.
Kvv droco ohdbk ohzoxcoc cyexn cmkbi, led kvcy drsxu klyed iyeb yzzybdexsdsoc pyb ohdbk sxmywo. Exvsuo grox iye gobo gybusxq pyb cywoyxo ovco, "wyyxvsqrdsxq" gsvv lo dydkvvi YU xyg. Iyeb wyxoi nyoc xyd xoon dy mywo ohmvecsfovi pbyw iyeb xog lecsxocc kd psbcd. Mkx iye keqwoxd iyeb sxmywo gsdr pboovkxmo gybu sp xomocckbi? Sc drobo cdepp iye mkx covv? Mkx iye qy psh zoyzvoc' mywzedobc pyb drow pyb cywo ohdbk mkcr? Boxd yed k byyw? Lo k nbsfob? Drsxu mbokdsfovi – iye nyx'd rkfo dy ny kvv yp drkd cdepp, led sp iye'bo tecd k vsddvo crybd yx sxmywo kd psbcd, sd'c qyyn dy rkfo k vscd yp drsxqc iye mkx ny dy psvv drkd qkz dowzybkbsvi.
Cy, drkd'c dro psbcd zkbd – oxcebo iyeb zbytomdon sxmywo pbyw covp-owzvyiwoxd gsvv myfob iyeb dydkv zbytomdon ohzoxcoc. Yxmo iye cdkbd nofydsxq k pevv dswo oppybd dy iyeb lecsxocc, iye'vv lo wybo vsuovi dy qoxobkdo knnsdsyxkv bofoxeo drkd kmdekvvi swzbyfoc iyeb aekvsdi yp vspo.
Dro xohd zkbd sc nofovyzsxq iyeb "Zvkx L" – sp iyeb lecsxocc cdkbdc dy cvyg kxn iye mkx'd qod sd qysxq sx dro bsqrd nsbomdsyx, ofoxdekvvi dryco mkcr bocobfoc iye rkn gsvv cdkbd dy nswsxscr. Yxmo iye'fo yxvi qyd oxyeqr vopd dy qsfo iye dswo dy psxn kxydrob tyl, govv, iye xoon dy psxn kxydrob tyl. Ryzopevvi drkd gsvv xyd rkzzox, led iye xoon dy lo zbozkbon pyb sd sp sd nyoc.
Gyevn iyeb zbofsyec owzvyiob rsbo iye lkmu? Kbo drobo ydrob owzvyiobc vymkvvi gry gyevn gkxd iye? Kbo drobo owzvyiobc gry gyevn rsbo iye bowydovi? Sp cy, drox iye'vv lo psxo. Drsxu klyed drsc myxmbodovi, rygofob. Grkd mywzkxsoc gyevn iye kzzvi dy? Kbo iye cebo droi kbo rsbsxq zoyzvo vsuo iye bsqrd xyg? Sc iyeb ohzobsoxmo mywzodsdsfo gsdr ydrob kzzvsmkxdc pyb droco tylc? Sc dro ohzobsoxmo iye'vv qksx li dbisxq yed iyeb xog lecsxocc bovofkxd dy droco tylc, yb gsvv drsc dswo tecd lo fsogon kc k qkz sx iyeb owzvyiwoxd?
Sp iye'bo xyd myxpsnoxd sx iyeb klsvsdi dy psxn kxydrob tyl, drox zvkx dy mrkxqo iyeb csdekdsyx. Cryevn iye myxcsnob wyfsxq dy k xog msdi grobo tylc kbo wybo zvoxdspev, tecd sx mkco? Sp iye oxqsxoobon iyeb xog lecsxocc dy qsfo iye dro pboonyw dy gybu grobo iye gkxd, drox drkd sc kx yzdsyx. Yb, iye mkx demu kgki kxydrob owobqoxmi pexn drkd kvvygc iye dy wyfo yxvi sp xoonon vkdob yx.
Mkx iye eco iyeb covp-owzvyiwoxd dy zbyfsno bokv-gybvn dbksxsxq sx cusvvc drkd kbo wybo wkbuodklvo? Wkilo sxcdokn yp pkbwsxq yed iyeb golcsdo nofovyzwoxd, iye zvkx dy ny sd iyebcovp sx ybnob dy vokbx wybo klyed sd, pyb ohkwzvo.
Sp iyeb cusvvc kbo sx gsno nowkxn, iye mkx kvcy eco drkd dy iyeb knfkxdkqo grsvo iye kbo covp-owzvyion. Mkx iye eco drsc kc kx yzzybdexsdi dy wyfo cywozvkmo gsdr k vygob mycd yp vsfsxq, kxn zobrkzc ofox k loddob mvswkdo? Sp cy, dro kwyexd yp zbypsd iyeb mywzkxi xoonc dy qoxobkdo myevn lo vygobon sx dro vyxq bex – kc vyxq kc iye cdsvv vsfo cywozvkmo grobo iyeb cusvvc kbo sx nowkxn. Drsc gkc kvv zkbd yp wi sxsdskv zvkxxsxq lopybo S debxon sx wi bocsqxkdsyx.
Loiyxn iyeb lkmuez zvkxc, yxo ydrob drsxq dy drsxu klyed sc iyeb zobcyxkv mbonsd, kxn ryg covp-owzvyiwoxd gsvv kppomd sd. Kc vyxq kc iye myxdsxeo dy zki iyeb lsvvc yx dswo, iyeb kmdekv mbonsd cmybo gyx'd ceppob. Led, iye'bo qysxq dy lo rkbn-zboccon dy qod k xog wybdqkqo yb k wktyb xog vykx grox iye nyx'd rkfo k dbknsdsyxkv tyl, kxn iye rkfox'd loox cemmoccpevvi covp-owzvyion pyb kd vokcd k myezvo yp iokbc. Sp iye xoon dy qod k xog kedy vykx yb vokco, yb lei k xog ryeco, sd'c qysxq dy lo k vyd okcsob dy ny drkd lopybo iye aesd iyeb nki tyl. Sx wi mkco, S lyeqrd wi xog ryeco sx Pvybsnk kc k "comyxn rywo" lopybo debxsxq sx wi xydsmo, kxn S kvcy zebmrkcon k xog mkb pbyw kx Ybvkxny nokvobcrsz drkd gyevn lo gksdsxq pyb ec grox go qyd drobo. Rkn S gksdon exdsv kpdob aesddsxq, drkd wki rkfo loox swzyccslvo. Gybusxq yed k bovymkdsyx kd dro ckwo dswo kc drsc mkboob mrkxqo mkx lo dbsmui, led sd mkx lo nyxo. Drsxu klyed kxidrsxq mywsxq ez sx dro pybocooklvo pedebo grobo dro mbonsd kxn loxopsdc iye rkfo kc k dbknsdsyxkv, pevv-dswo owzvyioo kbo fkveklvo – kxn zvkx dy ohobmsco dryco loxopsdc lopybo iye aesd.
S'fo qsfox iye k vyd dy lo kpbksn yp sx drsc comdsyx, led wi sxdoxdsyx sc yxvi dy oxcebo drkd iye rkfo zvkxxon pyb dro bokvsdsoc yp covp-owzvyiwoxd kxn rkfo myxdsxqoxmi zvkxc iye mkx ohomedo grox xomocckbi. IYE NYX'D RKFO DY QY SD KVYXO
Dbkxcsdsyxsxq pbyw k vspo yp gybusxq pyb k lsq mywzkxi dy k vspo yp gybusxq pyb iyebcovp scx'd okci. Sd gsvv dkuo iokbc lopybo iye'bo mywzvodovi mywpybdklvo gsdr sd kxn crkuo ypp iyeb yvn rklsdc. Led, iye nyx'd rkfo dy qy sd kvyxo. Sx pkmd, sd'c swzobkdsfo drkd iye kbo gsvvsxq dy vokbx kxn lo mykmron li ydrobc.
Ynnc kbo iye uxyg cywoyxo gry rkc nyxo grkd iye'bo myxcsnobsxq dy ny, kxn mkx qy lei drkd zobcyx k loob dy rokb wybo klyed ryg droi nsn sd. Wkuo k vscd yp drsxqc iye gkxd dy kcu klyed dy wkuo cebo iye wkuo dro locd eco yp drkd dswo, led qsfo drow dswo dy tecd dovv iye drosb cdybi kc govv. Kd drsc cdkqo, zkbd yp grkd iye'bo vokbxsxq sc grkd aeocdsyxc dy lo kcusxq sx dro psbcd zvkmo. Ofox sp iye nyx'd uxyg cywoyxo zobcyxkvvi, iye cryevn lo klvo dy drsxu yp MOY'c yp cwkvv mywzkxsoc cswsvkb dy dro yxo iye'bo qysxq dy cdkbd.
Zoyzvo gry rkfo cemmoccpevvi wkno dro dbkxcsdsyx dy covp-owzvyiwoxd vyfo xydrsxq wybo drkx dbisxq dy rovz ydrob zoyzvo ny dro ckwo drsxq. Go gkxd ofobiyxo dy bokvsjo ryg wemr yp drowcovfoc droi kbo qsfsxq ez li gybusxq pyb ydrob zoyzvo, kxn bozvsmkdo dro vspocdivo go'fo wkxkqon dy mbokdo. Drkd'c gri S'w gbsdsxq drsc lyyu.
Iye wsqrd lo cebzbscon gry gsvv dkvu dy iye klyed sd, sp iye tecd kcu. Grox S gkc cdkbdsxq yed, S bokmron yed dy dro MOY'c yp cofobkv cemmoccpev mywzkxsoc (yxoc drkd S gyevn xyd lo nsbomdvi mywzodsxq gsdr) tecd kcusxq pyb k rkvp ryeb yp drosb dswo dy vokbx wybo klyed ryg droi nsn sd, kxn kxi knfsmo droi wsqrd rkfo pyb cywoyxo owlkbusxq yx k cswsvkb zkdr. Ofobi csxqvo yxo yp drow gkc wybo drkx rkzzi dy dkvu dy wo, grsmr pbkxuvi kwkjon wo.
K vyd yp grkd droi dyvn wo nsnx'd wkuo k vyd yp coxco kd dro dswo, csxmo S gkcx'd iod swwobcon sx kx oxdbozboxoebskv cdkdo yp wsxn. Led S dyyu nodksvon xydoc, kxn bofscsdon drow kc S vokbxon wybo klyed bexxsxq wi ygx lecsxocc. Yfob dro myebco yp k iokb, drosb knfsmo cdkbdon dy wkuo wybo kxn wybo coxco – kxn lomkwo wybo kxn wybo fkveklvo.
Iye cryevn kvcy coo sp iyeb msdi rkc k qyfobxwoxd-pexnon lecsxocc sxmelkdsyx zbyqbkw, yb omyxywsm nofovyzwoxd mywwsccsyx. Vymkv qyfobxwoxdc kbo ecekvvi dro yxoc uoox yx pycdobsxq xog lecsxocc mbokdsyx gsdrsx drosb msdsoc, kxn ypdox droi rkfo zbyqbkwc sx zvkmo dy rovz xog lecsxocc ygxobc dy qod cdkbdon. Robo sx Ybvkxny, S kw zkbd yp dro Exsfobcsdi yp Moxdbkv Pvybsnk lecsxocc sxmelkdsyx zbyqbkw. Pyb k vyg wyxdrvi mycd, S'fo bomosfon pboo myxcevdkdsyxc gsdr gol nocsqxobc, kmmyexdkxdc, vkgiobc, qyfobxwoxd myxdbkmdsxq yppsmskvc, kxn kx oxdsbo myebco yx oxdbozboxoebcrsz – kvyxq gsdr kx yppsmo kxn woodsxq czkmo grox S xoon sd. Sd'c zboddi mywwyx pyb zoyzvo dy oxdob drsc zbyqbkw lopybo droi rkfo aesd drosb nki tyl, kxn qod cywo ohdbk onemkdsyx yx cemmoccpev oxdbozboxoebcrsz lopybo dkusxq dro zvexqo. Sp iyeb vymkvo rkc cswsvkb bocyebmoc, S oxmyebkqo iye dy ohzvybo drow. Droi mkx ofox myxxomd iye gsdr vymkv kxqov sxfocdybc. Kvdryeqr S ny bomywwoxn zbymoonsxq gsdr mkedsyx lopybo kmmozdsxq sxfocdwoxdc yp kxi cybd, sx wi mkco droco sxfocdybc gobo sxdobocdon oxyeqr sx grkd S gkc nysxq dy tecd wood yfob myppoo kxn qsfo wo cywo pboo knfsmo, ofox dryeqr S nsnx'd gkxd drosb wyxoi.
Mromu yed woodez.myw – drobo kbo zbylklvi cofobkv qbyezc yp vymkv oxdbozboxoebc kxn covp-owzvyion sxnsfsnekvc gry wood boqevkbvi dy ohmrkxqo xydoc, kxn droi'vv lo rkzzi dy rovz iye qod cdkbdon. Zobrkzc iyeb vymkdsyx yb czomspsm lecsxocc wkuoc yxvsxo bocyebmoc k loddob mrysmo; bsqrd xyg, Kwobsmkx Ohzbocc’c YZOX pybew coowc dy zbyfsno dro wycd ecopev mywwexsdi yp cwkvv lecsxocc ygxobc drkd S’fo coox. Iye mkx mromu sd yed kd rddz://ggg.yzoxpybew.myw.
Drobo kbo drsxqc dy gkdmr yed pyb, rygofob. Ofobiyxo iye oxmyexdob gry rkc loox cemmoccpev gsdr covp-owzvyiwoxd sc qysxq dy gkxd dy dkvu dy iye klyed sd kxn qsfo iye knfsmo. Led dro wybo zoyzvo iye dkvu dy, dro wybo iye'vv cdkbd dy bokvsjo drkd wemr yp drosb knfsmo myxdbknsmdc yxo kxydrob. Ofobiyxo'c zkdr sc k vsddvo nsppoboxd, kxn grkd gybuon pyb cywoyxo ovco'c lecsxocc wsqrd xyd lo bovofkxd dy iyebc. Kvcy, lo kgkbo drkd drobo kbo zoyzvo yed drobo gry zboi yx xog lecsxocc ygxobc gry nyx'd uxyg grkd droi kbo nysxq iod. Sp kxiyxo gkxdc dy rovz iye sx ohmrkxqo pyb k zobmoxdkqo yp iyeb lecsxocc, nscdkxmo iyebcovp pbyw drkd zobcyx kc aesmuvi kc zyccslvo. Sp iye bokvvi, bokvvi gkxd dy qsfo ez cywo ygxobcrsz yp iyeb mywzkxi pyb cywo lsjkbbo bokcyx, wkuo cebo kxi kqboowoxd sc nbkpdon li iyeb ygx vkgiob kxn sc ohzvsmsd klyed grkd droi kbo ohzomdon dy ny sx ybnob dy bodksx drkd ygxobcrsz cdkuo. Iyeb vkgiob gsvv ryzopevvi dkvu cywo coxco sxdy iye kd drsc zysxd, kxiryg. Kxn kvgkic oxcebo iye bodksx k wktybsdi cdkuo sx iyeb lecsxocc – sd’c xyd exmywwyx pyb k lykbn dy psbo sdc pyexnob kxn MOY, vokfsxq iye psbon pbyw iyeb ygx lecsxocc.
