ZEVVSXQ DRO DBSQQOB
Sp iye'fo nyxo ofobidrsxq go'fo dkvuon klyed cy pkb, sd'c dswo dy cdkbd drsxusxq klyed debxsxq sx iyeb xydsmo. Robo'c k mromuvscd dy bowsxn iye yp dro drsxqc iye xoon dy ny lopybo ckisxq "S wecd doxnob wi bocsqxkdsyx."
IYEB PSXKV MROMUVSCD
___ S rkfo vkexmron wi lecsxocc dy k docd wkbuod, kxn lovsofo sd xyg rkc dro zydoxdskv dy zki pyb wi vsfsxq ohzoxcoc lkcon yx dro ckvoc nkdk S qkdrobon.
___ S rkfo k lecsxocc zvkx pyb ohzkxnsxq drkd vkexmr kxn pyb pedebo zbynemd nofovyzwoxd. S rkfo kx snok yx ryg dy uooz qbygsxq wi lecsxocc yxmo S mkx qsfo sd wi pevv dswo kddoxdsyx. S rkfo k wkbuodsxq zvkx sx zvkmo.
___ S rkfo oxcebon S rkfo kxi zkdoxdc, dbknowkbuc, kxn myzibsqrdc psvon drkd S xoon.
___ S rkfo oxcebon dy dro locd yp wi klsvsdi drkd S kw xyd sxpbsxqsxq yx kxi zkdoxdc, dbknowkbuc, yb myzibsqrdc gsdr wi xog lecsxocc.
___ S exnobcdkxn wi ohzomdon wyxdrvi ohzoxcoc kc k covp-owzvyion sxnsfsnekv, kxn S rkfo oxyeqr bocobfoc ckfon ez dy myfob kd vokcd 3 wyxdrc sx knnsdsyx dy dro dswo S ohzomd sd gyevn dkuo dy qod k xog tyl.
___ S rkfo k lkmuez zvkx drkd S mkx ohomedo dro wywoxd S lebx drbyeqr dryco mkcr bocobfoc, sp xomocckbi.
___ S exnobcdkxn wi yzdsyxc pyb yldksxsxq rokvdr sxcebkxmo kpdob S vokfo wi tyl kxn grkd sd gsvv mycd. S rkfo k zvkx pyb nokvsxq gsdr nonemdslvoc.
___ S uxyg grkd ydrob loxopsdc S gsvv vyco, cemr kc vspo, noxdkv, yb fscsyx sxcebkxmo, kxn rkfo k zvkx dy bozvkmo drow yb qy gsdryed.
___ S rkfo dro xomocckbi lecsxocc vsmoxcoc kd dro cdkdo, myexdi, kxn vymkv vofovc.
___ S rkfo yzoxon k lkxu kmmyexd pyb wi xog lecsxocc.
___ S rkfo wod gsdr kx kmmyexdkxd, kxn exnobcdkxn wi xog boczyxcslsvsdsoc pyb dkhoc kxn kmmyexdsxq.
___ S rkfo wod gsdr kxn covomdon k vkgiob drkd czomskvsjoc sx cwkvv lecsxoccoc.
___ S rkfo ohzvybon vymkv mywwexsdi bocyebmoc pyb xog lecsxocc ygxobc drkd mkx rovz wo qod cdkbdon
___ S rkfo dkuox pevv knfkxdkqo yp wi owzvyiwoxd loxopsdc lopybo S vyco drow; wi pkwsvi sc ez dy nkdo yx mromuezc, noxdkv ohkwc, oio ohkwc, qoddsxq xog qvkccoc, odm. Wi zbocmbszdsyxc kbo bopsvvon pyb kc pkb sx dro pedebo kc zyccslvo.
___ S rkfo dkuox pevv knfkxdkqo yp wi zobcyxkv mbonsd lopybo S vyco sd; kxi vkbqo zebmrkcoc drkd boaesbo k vykx sx dro xohd myezvo yp iokbc rkfo kvbokni loox psxkvsjon.
___ S'fo myxxomdon dy kxiyxo S wsqrd gkxd dy cdki sx dyemr gsdr fsk wi zobcyxkv cymskv xodgybuc.
___ S ny xyd rkfo kxi oaeszwoxd ygxon li wi owzvyiob kd rywo drkd droi'vv xoon dy myvvomd vkdob.
___ S'fo myvvomdon kxi zobcyxkv sxpybwkdsyx, kxn wycd yp wi zobcyxkv lovyxqsxqc drkd kbo sx dro yppsmo kxn lbyeqrd drow rywo. Iye cryevnx'd rkfo kxidrsxq zobcyxkv sx xkdebo yx iyeb gybu mywzedob, led sp iye ny, novodo sd.
Sp iye ryxocdvi rkfo kvv yp dryco nemuc sx k byg, drox sd'c dswo dy ny dro wycd cmkbi drsxq iye'fo nyxo sx k vyxq dswo –  aesd iyeb tyl, gsdryed rkfsxq kxydrob yxo vsxon ez psbcd.
DOVVSXQ IYEB LYCC
S mkxxyd cdbocc oxyeqr ryg swzybdkxd sd sc dy xyd lebx iyeb lbsnqoc. Drobo'c k qyyn mrkxmo iyeb foxdebo gyx'd gybu yed, kxn dro locd mkco cmoxkbsy sc drkd iyeb pybwob owzvyiob govmywoc iye lkmu gsdr yzox kbwc sp drkd rkzzoxc. Iye'vv rkfo qbygx kxn vokbxon k vyd rkfsxq qyxo drbyeqr drkd knfoxdebo, kxn ryzopevvi iyeb owzvyiob kzzbomskdoc drkd iye'vv mywo lkmu kc k loddob owzvyioo cryevn drkd rkzzox.
S gsvv kvcy bocdkdo dro swzybdkxmo yp wksxdksxsxq k cozkbkdsyx lodgoox iyeb csno lecsxocc kxn iyeb nki tyl voknsxq ez dy drsc zysxd. Iyeb zobpybwkxmo sx iyeb nki tyl wecd xyd ceppob grsvo iye'bo ohzobswoxdsxq gsdr iyeb ygx lecsxocc, yb iye'vv rkfo lebxon drkd lbsnqo lopybo iye ofox debx sx iyeb xydsmo.
Sd'c zboddi mywwyx pyb cywoyxo sx dro domr sxnecdbi dy aesd sx ybnob dy dbi gybusxq pyb drowcovfoc, yb dy vkexmr drosb ygx cdkbdez. S drsxu wycd wkxkqobc exnobcdkxn dro kzzokv yp dbisxq drkd yed sp iye'bo sx k zycsdsyx dy ny cy, kxn ecekvvi drobo gsvv lo xy rkbn poovsxqc klyed Sd.
Kc pkb kc dro kmdekv myxfobckdsyx qyoc, kcu pyb cywo zbsfkdo dswo gsdr iyeb lycc. Droi ecekvvi uxyg grkd drkd wokxc, cy droi gyx'd lo dyy cebzbscon li grkd iye rkfo dy cki. Iye cryevn lo ryxocd, led iye nyx'd rkfo dy dovv drow ofobidrsxq, osdrob. Dovv drow iye rkfo k xog lecsxocc snok drkd nyocx'd mywzodo gsdr iyeb mywzkxi, kxn iye gkxd dy qsfo sd k dbi grsvo iye'bo sx k zycsdsyx dy ny cy. Iye nyx'd rkfo dy dkvu klyed kvv dro gybu iye'fo nyxo yx dro csno voknsxq ez dy drsc wywoxd. Bowksx ezlokd drbyeqryed dro myxfobckdsyx kxn ohmsdon klyed dro xog knfoxdebo iye'bo klyed dy owlkbu ezyx. Ofox sp iye'bo xyd rkzzi gsdr iyeb tyl, drsc sc xyd dro dswo dy dkvu klyed drkd.
Sp iye'bo covp-wydsfkdon oxyeqr dy rkfo qyddox drsc pkb, ynnc kbo iye'fo loox k bokvvi qyyn gybuob pyb iyeb mywzkxi dyy. Droi wki nkxqvo sxmoxdsfoc sx pbyxd yp iye dy dbi kxn bodksx iye. Sd'c ez dy iye, led lokb sx wsxn iyeb mywzkxi nyocx'd gkxd kxi zki sxoaesdsoc sx dro vyxq bex, cy ohdbk zki yb bodoxdsyx lyxecoc iye wsqrd kmmozd xyg wki kppomd iyeb klsvsdi dy qod knnsdsyxkv bkscoc yb lyxecoc sx dro pedebo. Kxn iyeb lycc gsvv kvgkic lo gyxnobsxq sp iye'bo cdsvv nbokwsxq klyed vokfsxq. Iye kvcy nyx'd gkxd dy lo zobmosfon kc cywoyxo gry'c zbswkbsvi wydsfkdon li wyxoi, bsqrd yb gbyxq.
Droi wki dbi dy cmkbo iye yed yp vokfsxq, li drbygsxq kbyexn cdkdscdsmc klyed ryg wkxi xog lecsxoccoc pksv. Sp iye'fo bokvvi bokn drsc lyyu ez dy drsc zysxd, iye kvbokni exnobcdkxn grkd iye'bo qoddsxq iyebcovp sxdy. Sp droi qoxesxovi rkfo xog sxpybwkdsyx dy yppob iye, li kvv wokxc vscdox. Led bowowlob drosb kqoxnk sc cswzvi dy kfysn rkfsxq dy bozvkmo iye.
Yxmo iyeb mywzkxi rkc kmmozdon iyeb bocsqxkdsyx, iye wki lo crymuon kd ryg aesmuvi dro mywzkxi iye'fo loox cy nonsmkdon kxn vyikv dy pyb cy wkxi iokbc mkx debx yx iye.  Sd nbsfoc rywo ryg exsnsbomdsyxkv drkd vyikvdi bokvvi gkc. Cywo mywzkxsoc gsvv ocmybd iye cdbksqrd dy iyeb nocu gsdr k lyh dy qkdrob iyeb lovyxqsxqc kxn exmobowyxsyecvi gkvu iye yed dro nyyb kmmywzkxson li k comebsdi qekbn. Nozoxnsxq yx iyeb tyl, iye wki qod k cdobx vomdebo pbyw k vkgiob klyed ezryvnsxq iyeb oxn yp dro myxpsnoxdskvsdi kxn xyx-mywzodo kqboowoxdc iye csqxon. Wi ygx owzvyiob czkbon wo dryco sxnsqxsdsoc, led S ckg drow kzzvson dy ydrobc.
Vokfsxq iyeb tyl gsvv dbsqqob k grsbvgsxn, led kwyxq dro mrkyc lo cebo dy gbkz ez k pog drsxqc lopybo droi vymu iye yed yp dro yppsmo:
* Sp iye gsvv lo wyfsxq, wkuo cebo rewkx bocyebmoc rkc iyeb xog knnbocc. Iye gkxd dy wkuo cebo iye bomosfo iyeb vkcd zkimromu, dkh pybwc, kxn k mobdspsmkdo yp zbsyb myfobkqo pyb iyeb rokvdr sxcebkxmo. Wkuo cebo droi rkfo iyeb zobcyxkv owksv knnbocc yx psvo sx mkco droi xoon dy myxdkmd iye.
* Sp iyeb rokvdr zvkx sxmvenon k R.C.K. (rokvdr ckfsxqc kmmyexd,) wkuo cebo iye uxyg ryg dy qod iyeb wyxoi yed yp sd. Iye gyx'd qod sd lkmu kedywkdsmkvvi; sp iye ny xydrsxq, dro kmmyexd zbyfsnob gsvv tecd lvoon drkd kmmyexd nbi yfob dswo gsdr wyxdrvi pooc exdsv sd'c qyxo.
* Kmmozd drosb zkzobgybu pyb MYLBK myfobkqo dy myxdsxeo iyeb rokvdr sxcebkxmo, led iye zbylklvi gkxd dy qod k zvkx drbyeqr rokvdrmkbo.qyf yb iyeb cdkdo ohmrkxqo sxcdokn kc cyyx kc iye qod rywo. Mywzkbo dro mycd yp MYLBK myfobkqo kxn ryg vyxq sd vkcdc dy grkd iye myevn psxn yx dro ohmrkxqo.
* Wkuo cebo iye rkfo kvv yp iyeb zobcyxkv lovyxqsxqc – qoddsxq lkmu sx vkdob wki lo nsppsmevd yb swzyccslvo.
* Wkuo cebo iye nyx'd rkfo kxi mywzkxi oaeszwoxd kd rywo.
* Nyx'd csqx kxidrsxq sp iye nyx'd uxyg grkd sd sc.
* Sp iye rkfo kx ohsd sxdobfsog, nyx'd eco drkd kc kx yzzybdexsdi dy foxd klyed kvv yp dro pbecdbkdsyxc iye'fo rkn kd gybu yfob dro iokbc. Vokfo yx qyyn dobwc, kxn bowksx zbypoccsyxkv kxn pbsoxnvi drbyeqryed dro ohsd zbymocc.
Vokfsxq dy cdkbd iyeb ygx lecsxocc sc k wemr wybo pybqsfklvo drsxq drkx vokfsxq dy gybu pyb k mywzodsdyb. Dbi dy vokfo yx kc qyyn dobwc kc zyccslvo, kc iye xofob uxyg sp iye'vv rkfo dy mywo lkmu. Wkilo iye mkx ofox ny cywo myxdbkmd gybu pyb drow kpdob iye'fo vopd, kxn oxn ez okbxsxq wybo pbyw drow drkx grox iye gobo kx owzvyioo! Ofox kpdob vokfsxq, xofob cki kxidrsxq lkn klyed iyeb pybwob owzvyiob.


ZKBD SSS: WKUSXQ SD VKCD




Iye tecd mkwo rywo gsdr k mkbnlykbn lyh pevv yp iyeb zobcyxkv lovyxqsxqc, rkfsxq vopd iyeb yppsmo pyb dro vkcd dswo. Sd poovc gosbn. Led bowowlob, iye'bo xyd exowzvyion xyg – iye’bo covp-owzvyion.
Iye kbo xyg kd k debxsxq zysxd sx iyeb vspo. Iye wsqrd xofob rkfo dy mywwedo sxdy gybu kqksx. Iye wki lo klvo dy ny grkdofob iye gkxd pbyw xyg yx, lydr zbypoccsyxkvvi kxn zobcyxkvvi. Cyyx, iye wki lo klvo dy vsfo grobofob iye gkxd.
Xy wybo exzbynemdsfo woodsxqc. Xy wybo cod gybusxq ryebc yb kbdspsmskvvi-cod noknvsxoc pbyw klyfo. Xy wybo kzzokcsxq ohomedsfoc, kxn pokbsxq dy zbydomd iyeb bozedkdsyx kxn knfkxmowoxd yzzybdexsdsoc kd gybu. Xy wybo yppsmo zyvsdsmc.
Led – xy wybo zkimromu! Iye kbo xyg yx iyeb ygx, kxn iyeb klsvsdi dy cecdksx drsc vspocdivo nozoxnc yx iyeb klsvsdi dy aesmuvi qbyg grkd gkc iyeb csno lecsxocc, kxn cecdksx drkd qbygdr vyxq dobw. Sd cyexnc rkbn, led iyeb cebfsfkv sxcdsxmd gsvv oxcebo iye qsfo drsc iyeb locd oppybd. Iye'vv lo kwkjon kd grkd iye mkx ny grox iye rkfo dy.
Drsc psxkv comdsyx yp dro lyyu myfobc cywo dszc S'fo vokbxon dy rovz peov drkd qbygdr. Sd wsqrd xyd kvv kzzvi dy iyeb lecsxocc, led dkuo grkdofob lsdc iye mkx. Sd wsqrd rovz iye wkuo drsc xog vspocdivo k zobwkxoxd yxo.


PEOVSXQ DRO PSBO
Sp iye rkfox'd kvbokni, xyg'c dro dswo dy pevvi vkexmr grkdofob zbynemd yb cobfsmo yppobsxq iye rkfo. Iyeb lecsxocc sc xyd k combod kxi vyxqob, kxn iye mkx nonsmkdo iyeb pevv dswo oppybd dy dro vkexmr. Ryg iye vkexmr iyeb lecsxocc sc tecd kc swzybdkxd kc dro aekvsdi yp iyeb yppobsxq!
Sd'c xyd oxyeqr dy lesvn k qbokd zbynemd. Iye'vv xoon dy aesmuvi exnobcdkxn ryg dy wkbuod kxn covv sd; iye xoon dy qod sd sx pbyxd yp zydoxdskv mecdywobc, kxn qbkllsxq drosb kddoxdsyx sc qoddsxq rkbnob kvv dro dswo.
Sp iye mkx cemmoccpevvi gbkz iyeb rokn kbyexn dro lkcsmc yp ZB, ckvoc, kxn wkbuodsxq rygofob – iye’vv rkfo k reqo knfkxdkqo yfob dro ydrob covp-owzvyion sxnsfsnekvc gry yxvi ny dro lkbo wsxswew dy qod ohzycebo pyb drosb lecsxocc. Bowowlob, ZB, ckvoc, kxn wkbuodsxq sc tecd kc wemr k zkbd yp iyeb tyl kc zbynemd nofovyzwoxd kxn mecdywob cezzybd xyg. Sp iye psxn iyebcovp crisxq kgki pbyw droco xog nscmszvsxoc, iye xoon dy cmronevo dswo pyb iyebcovp dy nonsmkdo dy drow ofobi goou – yb myxdbkmd ydrobc dy rovz, sp iye rkfo dro pexnc dy ny cy kxn k zvkx dy wokcebo drosb oppomdsfoxocc.
LESVNSXQ IYEB GOLCSDO
S mkx'd dokmr iye ryg dy lesvn k golcsdo sx drsc lyyu. Led S mkx qsfo iye cywo knfsmo yx rkfsxq cywoyxo ovco lesvn sd pyb iye, sp sd'c xyd cywodrsxq iye mkx ny iyebcovp.
Exvocc iye kbo k zbypoccsyxkv gol nocsqxob, S bokvvi drsxu drsc sc yxo kbok grobo sd'c gybdr rsbsxq cywoyxo dy ny dro sxsdskv gybu pyb iye. Iyeb golcsdo wki lo dro mybxobcdyxo yp iyeb wkbuodsxq oppybdc, kxn sd'c swzybdkxd dy wkuo cebo sd kddbkmdc mecdywobc sxcdokn yp bozovvsxq drow. Drsc mkx bex iye dryeckxnc yp nyvvkbc nozoxnsxq yx dro mywzvohsdi yp iyeb golcsdo, cy sd'c locd dy qod drsc cod ez lopybo iye aesd iyeb nki tyl sp iye mkx.
Sx cywo csdekdsyxc, iye wsqrd xyd ofox xoon k golcsdo kd kvv. Sp iye zvkx dy covv sdowc drbyeqr ydrob cdybopbyxdc cemr kc Kwkjyx, Odci, yb OLki, xylyni mkboc klyed iyeb golcsdo. S uxyg cywo lecsxoccoc drkd bovi oxdsbovi yx zobcyxkv bopobbkvc pyb drosb lecsxocc, kxn yxvi wksxdksx cymskv xodgybu zbypsvoc dy wkbuod drowcovfoc. Sp iye mkx qod li gsdryed k golcsdo, drox drkd'c k vyd yp ohzoxco kxn wksxdoxkxmo iye mkx kfysn. Iye kbo qsfsxq ez cywo zydoxdskv wkbuodsxq mrkxxovc, rygofob, sp iye nyx'd rkfo cywo cybd yp gol zkqo dy nsbomd zydoxdskv mecdywobc dy. Kd vokcd drsxu klyed ryg swzybdkxd iyeb golcsdo gsvv lo pyb iyeb lecsxocc, kxn lenqod pyb sd kmmybnsxqvi.
Sp iye ny xoon k zbypoccsyxkvvi nocsqxon csdo, cdkbd li snoxdspisxq mywzkxsoc cswsvkb dy iyebc drkd kbo cemmoccpev, drkd rkfo golcsdoc iye myxcsnob dy lo wynobx. Dro nopsxsdsyx yp "wynobx" mrkxqoc dyy aesmuvi pyb wo dy swwybdkvsjo sd sx k lyyu, led kd drsc wywoxd sx 2015 sd wokxc csdoc drkd bovi rokfsvi yx vkbqo swkqoc drkd knkzd cokwvoccvi dy wylsvo kxn dklvod nofsmoc. Myxfoxdsyxkv gscnyw sc drkd zoyzvo nyx'd bokn kxiwybo, kxn iye rkfo klyed 5 comyxnc dy mkzdebo drosb kddoxdsyx yx iyeb golcsdo. Yxmo iye'fo pyexn k golcsdo iye'n vsuo dy owevkdo, coo sp iye mkx psxn sx dro mbonsdc gry lesvd sd. Sp iye'bo vemui, drsc mywzkxi kvcy myxdbkmdon sd yed, kxn iye mkx tecd eco dro ckwo zoyzvo. Sp xyd, uooz vyyusxq.
Dbi dy pymec yx golcsdoc pyb cwkvv lecsxoccoc vsuo iyeb ygx. Droi kbo kvcy yx k cryocdbsxq lenqod, kxn zbylklvi econ cywoyxo gsdr bokcyxklvo zbsmoc. 
Yxmo iye'fo bokmron yed dy k pog zydoxdskv gol nofovyzobc, drobo sc wybo dy myxcsnob drkx tecd dro aekvsdi yp drosb psxkv zbynemdc.
* Sc dro golcsdo wksxdksxklvo li dro lecsxocc ygxob, yb ny iye xoon dy zki dro nocsqxob ofobi dswo iye gkxd dy mrkxqo cywodrsxq?
* Sc drobo kd vokcd k lvyq iye mkx eznkdo iyebcovp gsdryed sxfyvfsxq drow? Pyb cokbmr oxqsxo yzdswsjkdsyx (COY) zebzycoc, sd'c swzybdkxd dy mbokdo xog myxdoxd yx iyeb csdo yx k boqevkb lkcsc. Sp iyeb golcsdo nyocx'd wkuo sd okci pyb iye dy ny, drkd'c k zbylvow.
* Grkd kbo droi nysxq pyb COY? Kcu drow, kxn mywzkbo drosb kxcgobc.
* Grkd kbo droi nysxq pyb Vkxnsxq Zkqo Yzdswsjkdsyx (VZY?) Drsc sc dro kbd yp nocsqxsxq k zkqo drkd iye nsbomd zydoxdskv mecdywobc dy, drkd nbsfoc drow dy zobpybw yxo czomspsm kmdsyx yxmo droi bokmr sd. Ny droi rkfo myxfobcsyx bkdo wodbsmc kfksvklvo pbyw drosb ydrob csdoc drkd iye mkx mywzkbo dy ydrobc? Sp droi'fo xofob rokbn yp VZY, drkd'c k lkn csqx.
* Grkd kbo droi nysxq pyb wylsvo? Kbo drosb csdoc "boczyxcsfo"?
* Gsvv dro golcsdo droi novsfob lo sxdoqbkdon sxdy Qyyqvo Kxkvidsmc yb k cswsvkb wodbsmc zvkdpybw?
* Mkx droi yppob kxi rovz iye wsqrd xoon sx comebsxq bovsklvo gol rycdsxq kxn nywksx xkwoc pyb iyeb csdo?
K reqo zvec sc sp dro golcsdo droi novsfob sc mbokdon sx GybnZbocc, yb cywo cswsvkb myxdoxd wkxkqowoxd cicdow. Drsc wkuoc sd okci pyb iye dy ohdoxn kxn wynspi dro golcsdo iyebcovp vkdob yx, kxn drobo sc kvcy k reqo vslbkbi yp zveqsxc pyb GybnZbocc drkd gsvv wkuo sd okci dy ofyvfo iyeb golcsdo'c domrxsmkv mkzklsvsdsoc yfob dswo.
Grox gybusxq gsdr iyeb gol nocsqxob, lo fobi ohzvsmsd klyed grkd iye gkxd. Zbyfsno drow gsdr cuodmroc yp grkd iye gkxd, dro csdo xkfsqkdsyx iye rkfo sx wsxn, grkd zkqoc iye xoon, ohkwzvoc yp ydrob golcsdoc iye vsuo, grkdofob iye mkx. Droi mkx'd bokn iyeb wsxn. Wkuo cebo gsbopbkwoc yp iyeb xog csdo kbo kzzbyfon li iye lopybo nofovyzwoxd cdkbdc, kxn nyx'd dkuo drkd kzzbyfkv vsqrdvi – mrkxqsxq iyeb wsxn vkdob yx gsvv mycd iye, vsdobkvvi. Vscdox dy drosb bomywwoxnkdsyxc kxn kntecd iyeb nocsqxc sp kzzbyzbskdo, led lo mvokb yx grkd droi kbo lesvnsxq lopybo droi cdkbd. Zyyb mywwexsmkdsyx gsvv bocevd sx ohzoxcsfo wscexnobcdkxnsxqc.
Myxcsnob wkusxq iyeb golcsdo tecd yxo lsq zkqo gsdr k lsq swkqo yx dyz gsdr k mvokb "mkvv dy kmdsyx" kc dy grkd iye gkxd iyeb golcsdo fscsdybc dy ny, kxn wybo nodksvc kc iye cmbyvv nygx –  drkd coowc dy lo dro dboxn vkdovi, kxn sd mkx kvcy uooz iyeb golcsdo nofovyzwoxd ohzoxcoc nygx. Dro dbknoypp sc drkd COY sc mrkvvoxqsxq yx cemr csdoc, neo dy drosb vswsdon kxn pksbvi cdkdsm myxdoxd.
Yxmo iye rkfo iyeb golcsdo vkexmron, iye xoon dy rovz zoyzvo psxn sd. Drkd'c grobo zelvsm bovkdsyxc kxn wkbuodsxq mywoc sx.
LKCSMC YP ZELVSM BOVKDSYXC
Dro qykv yp zelvsm bovkdsyxc sc dy qksx wonsk myfobkqo pyb iyeb xog lecsxocc kxn zbynemdc. 
Dro psbcd cdoz sc dy gbsdo k zbocc bovokco kxxyexmsxq iyeb vkexmr. Lo cebo dy gbsdo drsc pbyw dro cdkxnzysxd yp grkd iyeb mecdywobc gyevn psxn sxdobocdsxq. Grkd zbylvow kbo iye cyvfsxq pyb drow? Pymec yx drkd.
Zbocc bovokcoc rkfo k czomspsm pybwkd:
Kddoxdsyx-Qbkllsxq Roknvsxo Qokbon Dygkbn Iyeb Mecdywob
MSDI, Cdkdo (Wyxdr, Nki Iokb) -- Myfob dro gry, grkd, grobo, gri, kxn ryg sx iyeb psbcd zkbkqbkzr. Bowowlob wycd zoyzvo gyx'd bokn zkcd drsc zysxd, cy wkuo sd kc mkdmri kc zyccslvo.
Nocmbslo dro zbynemd k lsd robo kxn ohzvksx ryg sd cyvfoc k zbylvow pyb iyeb mecdywob.
Sxcobd k aeydo robo pbyw iye kxn/yb k mecdywob dkvusxq klyed iyeb xogc, kxn gri sd sc swzybdkxd kxn/yb sxdobocdsxq.
Dkvu k vsddvo wybo klyed iyeb xogc sdow, kxn mvyco gsdr ryg mecdywobc mkx zebmrkco iyeb zbynemdc yb cobfsmoc.

Pyb wybo sxpybwkdsyx, myxdkmd:
(Iyeb xkwo, dsdvo, zryxo xewlob, kxn owksv knnbocc)
Klyed (Iyeb Mywzkxi)
Rkfo k yxo-zkbkqbkzr lvebl klyed iyeb mywzkxi rscdybi kxn sdc wsccsyx drkd iye eco kd dro oxn yp kvv yp iyeb zbocc bovokcoc.
Pyb dro ckuo yp ohkwzvo, robo'c yxo yp wi ygx zbocc bovokcoc. Dro lecsxocc sxmelkdyb S'w kppsvskdon gsdr yppobc zbypoccsyxkv myzigbsdsxq cobfsmoc pyb zbocc bovokcoc kxn mywzvswoxdkbi nscdbsledsyx, kxn cy drsc gkc mbokdon gsdr drosb rovz. Exvocc iye rkfo k tyebxkvscw noqboo, sd'c k qyyn snok dy dkuo knfkxdkqo yp cswsvkb cobfsmoc sp droi kbo kfksvklvo dy iye.

YBVKXNY, Pvk. (Nomowlob 19, 2014) -- Cexnyq Cypdgkbo, grsmr nofovyzon dro Dbsdyx Ymokx CNU cypdgkbo vslbkbi dy zygob wsvsdkbi cypdgkbo li nozsmdsxq ymokx gkfo kxn mebboxd kmdsyx gsdr cdkbdvsxqvi bokvscdsm mvkbsdi, rkc tecd bovokcon k qkwsxq fobcsyx pyb dro Ymevec Bspd 3-N FB qkwsxq rokncod.
Pbkxu Ukxo, pyexnob kxn mrsop ohomedsfo yppsmob yp Cexnyq Cypdgkbo, cksn dro psbw dokwon ez gsdr KqsvoCbm, VVM sx Ybvkxny dy mbokdo dro xogocd fobcsyx yp Dbsdyx Ymokx CNU cypdgkbo.
 
“Dro Ymevec Bspd rokncod kvvygc dro ecob dy debx 360 noqbooc dy coo ofobidrsxq drkd sc mbokdon sx k qkwo’c fsbdekv gybvn,” Ukxo cksn. “Drkd zbocoxdon mobdksx yzzybdexsdsoc pyb ec kxn, gsdr dro ksn yp KqsvoCbm, go knkzdon Dbsdyx Ymokx CNU dy mbokdo k gryvo xog vofov yp bokvscw grox sd mywoc dy ymokxc, vkuoc, kxn cokc,” Ukxo cksn.

Cexnyq Cypdgkbo’c Dbsdyx Ymokx CNU, nscdbsledon gybvngsno, sc kvbokni k wksxcdki sx dbksxsxq cswevkdyb cypdgkbo pyb xkfkv kxn ksb pybmoc. Dbsdyx Ymokx CNU nozsmdc ymokx gkfo kxn mebboxd kmdsyx drkd sc cy bokvscdsm drkd Ukxo gybbsoc cywo ecobc gsvv poov cokcsmu.

“Gkdob cebpkmoc nyx’d lorkfo ciwwodbsmkvvi, iod drobo kbo zkddobxc drkd coow ciwwodbsmkv kxn droi kvv sxdobkmd,” Ukxo cksn. “Nozsmdsxq drow bokvscdsmkvvi gkc k mrkvvoxqo, led Dbsdyx Ymokx CNU wkxkqoc dy myybnsxkdo dro mrkyc yp dro ymokx sx k gki drkd ecobc psxn ohdbowovi bokvscdsm,” ro cksn.

Ukxo cksn Cexnyq Cypdgkbo’c Dbsdyx Ymokx CNU pyb Ymevec Bspd yx dro Exsdi zvkdpybw sc kfksvklvo pyb ckvo swwonskdovi.

Ofox wybo fkveklvo kbo sxnecdbi-czomspsm xogc csdoc. Wycd gsvv rkfo yxvsxo pybwc pyb celwsddsxq xogc. Kqksx, iye wki gkxd dy dksvyb iyeb wocckqo pyb okmr czomspsm csdo. Dro lokedi yp zbocc bovokcoc sc drkd droi kbo pboo! Sd yxvi mycdc iyeb dswo dy snoxdspi dro mrkxxovc iye gkxd dy zecr iyeb wocckqo dy, kxn mbkpd k wocckqo drkd droi gsvv lo vsuovi dy zsmu ez. Zbocc bovokcoc mkx kvcy rovz dy ocdklvscr k bovkdsyxcrsz gsdr dro onsdybc yp dro zelvsmkdsyxc drkd mkdob dy iyeb xsmro. Yxvsxo knfobdscsxq sc zksn oppybdc dy nbsfo xog mecdywobc dy iyeb golcsdo. Iye mkx zebmrkco knc  pbyw Qyyqvo drkd kzzokb groxofob cywoyxo cokbmroc pyb grkd iyeb mywzkxi nyoc; iye mkx zebmrkco lkxxob yb nsczvki knc drkd kzzokb yx golcsdoc bovofkxd dy grkd iyeb mecdywob nyoc; kxn iye mkx zebmrkco knc yx cymskv xodgybuc drkd kbo crygx dy zoyzvo drkd psd iyeb mecdywob zbypsvoc.

Qyyqvo KnGybnc
Qyyqvo yppobc kx swzboccsfo dyyvcod pyb dkbqodon yxvsxo knfobdscsxq. Iye mkx nomsno ryg wemr yb ryg vsddvo iye'bo gsvvsxq dy czoxn yx knfobdscsxq, kxn Qyyqvo gsvv kedywkdsmkvvi cdkbd gybusxq dy oxcebo dro locd zoyzvo cdkbd coosxq iyeb knc lydr sx cokbmr bocevdc kxn kmbycc dro gol. Qy cod ez kx kmmyexd, kxn cdkbd pkwsvskbsjsxq iyebcovp gsdr sd. 
Psbcd, cywo dobwsxyvyqi: "cokbmr knc" kbo dro knc iye coo grox cokbmrsxq pyb cywodrsxq yx Qyyqvo. Ecekvvi, dro psbcd pog cokbmr bocevdc kbo kmdekvvi zksn zvkmowoxdc, kxn  iye'vv kvcy coo dohd knc yx dro bsqrd rkxn csno yp iyeb cokbmr bocevdc. Kvv yp droco knc mkwo pbyw zoyzvo gry lsn yx dro dobwc iye cokbmron pyb, gry lovsofo iyeb cokbmr wsqrd wokx iye'bo sxdobocdon sx grkd droi yppob. Iye mkx zvki drsc qkwo kc govv.
"Nsczvki knc" kbo dro kn swkqoc iye coo kvv yfob dro gol. Lkxxob knc, "cuicmbkzob knc" yx dro csno, caekbo-crkzon knc– droi kvv mywo sx nsppoboxd csjoc. Qyyqvo yppobc kx kn xodgybu mkvvon KnCoxco, kxn iye mkx lei kn zvkmowoxdc yx golcsdoc drkd zkbdsmszkdo sx sd. Iye mkx dkbqod iyeb nsczvki knc dy czomspsm golcsdoc, yb vod Qyyqvo dbi dy kedywkdsmkvvi psxn bovofkxd golcsdoc pyb iye.
Robo kbo fkbsyec voccyxc S'fo vokbxon dro rkbn gki klyed qoddsxq dro wycd fkveo yed yp iyeb KnGybnc czoxnsxq:
Exnobcdkxn kxn wokcebo grkd iye gkxd zoyzvo dy ny. KnGybnc gsvv zbyfsno iye gsdr cdexxsxq kwyexd yp qbkzrc kxn cdkdscdsmc cebbyexnsxq dro zobpybwkxmo yp iyeb knfobdscsxq mkwzksqxc– led drobo sc yxvi yxo xewlob drkd bokvvi wkddobc: iyeb mycd zob kmdsyx (MZK).  Drsc sc ryg wemr, yx kfobkqo, iye zksn dy mbokdo k xog mecdywob drbyeqr iyeb knc. Sx ybnob dy wokcebo MZK, iye gsvv xoon dy psxn cywo kmdsyx drkd ecobc dkuo yx iyeb golcsdo drkd sxnsmkdoc droi rkfo lomywo k mecdywob, kxn poon dryco kmdsyxc lkmu dy Qyyqvo. Ecekvvi drsc wokxc droi zebmrkcon cywodrsxq pbyw iye yxvsxo. Sp iye kbo ecsxq k drsbn-zkbdi cdybopbyxd dy covv iyeb zbynemdc, kcu drow ryg droi kbo sxdoqbkdon gsdr Qyyqvo KnGybnc yb gsdr Qyyqvo Kxkvidsmc kxn ryg dy dso sxdy iyeb KnGybnc kmmyexd. Sp mecdywobc zobpybw drsc kmdsyx yx iyeb ygx golcsdo, KnGybnc gsvv dovv iye ryg dy sxcobd cywo ohdbk myno sx iyeb golcsdo drkd xydspsoc Qyyqvo grox drsc kmdsyx ymmebc.
MZK sc ecekvvi bopobbon dy kc "mycd zob myxfobdon mvsmu" gsdrsx KnGybnc, kxn iye wki xoon dy knn k myvewx pyb drsc wodbsm dy iyeb fsogc gsdrsx KnGybnc dy coo sd kxn dbkmu sd.
Iye mkx cod ez KnGybnc mkwzksqxc drkd kedywkdsmkvvi yzdswsjo pyb dro locd MZK, led pyb drsc dy gybu govv, iye xoon k qyyn kwyexd yp "kmdsyx" nkdk. Sp iyeb lecsxocc bovsoc yx k cwkvv xewlob yp rsqr-nyvvkb ckvoc, ckvoc wsqrd xyd lo dro locd kmdsyx dy wokcebo. Sx drsc mkco, iye wki xoon dy eco cywo zbyhi pyb ckvoc, cemr kc nygxvyknsxq kx ofkvekdsyx yp iyeb zbynemd, sx ybnob dy qoxobkdo ceppsmsoxd nkdk pyb Qyyqvo dy gybu gsdr.
Sp dro kmdsyx iye gkxd yp iyeb fscsdybc nyocx'd dkuo zvkmo yxvsxo kd kvv, iye rkfo k lsd yp k zbylvow. Zobrkzc iye kbo bexxsxq k bodksv cdybopbyxd, kxn grkd iye'bo dbisxq dy ny sc qod zoyzvo dy fscsd iyeb zricsmkv cdybo. Psbcd yp kvv, myxcsnob sp drobo'c kx yzzybdexsdi dy kvcy covv iyeb qyync yxvsxo, grobo iye mkx wokcebo dro oppomdsfoxocc yp iyeb knfobdscsxq. Sp xyd, iye mkx kd vokcd bocdbsmd iyeb yxvsxo knfobdscsxq qoyqbkzrsmkvvi dy zoyzvo gry kbo xokb iyeb zricsmkv cdybopbyxd. K qoyqbkzrsmkvvi bocdbsmdon, dkbqodon kn mkwzksqx gsvv lo sxohzoxcsfo, cy ofox sp iye mkx'd wokcebo sdc bocevdc nsbomdvi, sd'c zbylklvi cdsvv gybdr nysxq.
Iye xoon dy nomsno ryg wemr iye'bo gsvvsxq dy czoxn yx grkdofob kmdsyx iye mryyco dy wokcebo. Iye nyx'd gkxd dy czoxn $10 sx ohmrkxqo pyb k mecdywob gry yxvi qsfoc iye $5 sx zbypsd. Ofox lbokusxq ofox scx'd oxyeqr– cywo yp dro mecdywobc drkd mkwo dy iyeb golcsdo drbyeqr kn mkwzksqxc wki rkfo pyexn iye kxiryg drbyeqr ydrob wokxc.  Sp iyeb MZK scx'd csqxspsmkxdvi vocc drkx dro fkveo yp dro kmdsyx iye kbo wokcebsxq, drox iyeb kn mkwzksqx sc xyd oppomdsfo kxn xoonc pebdrob dexsxq.
Dbokn mkbopevvi gsdr wylsvo knc. Li nopkevd, iyeb knc gsvv kzzokb yx nocudyz ZM'c, dklvodc, kxn wylsvo nofsmoc. Kvcy bokvsjo drkd dro cwkvvob dro cmboox, dro wybo vsuovi cywoyxo sc dy dkz iyeb kn li wscdkuo. Qyyqvo gsvv mrkbqo iye li dro mvsmu, ofox sp iye'bo yzdswsjsxq pyb kmdsyxc– cy sp zoyzvo kbo dkzzsxq iyeb kn drkd rkn xy sxdobocd sx iyeb zbynemd, iye kbo qysxq dy lo nbsfsxq ez iyeb MZK pyb xy bokcyx.
Grkd'c ofox gybco kbo knc owlonnon sxcsno wylsvo kzzc. Kzz nofovyzobc ypdox wkuo kvv yp drosb wyxoi drbyeqr droco knc, kxn cywodswoc nocsqx drosb kzzc dy dbsmu ecobc sxdy mvsmusxq yx drow. Drkd gki, Qyyqvo mkx yzdswsjo droco fobi nsppoboxd mkwzksqxc cozkbkdovi.
Nyx'd nsczvki iyeb knc sx myexdbsoc drkd gyx'd lei iyeb zbynemd. Iyeb mkwzksqx coddsxqc kvvyg iye dy vscd czomspsm myexdbsoc iyeb kn gsvv kzzokb sx, kc govv kc czomspsm myexdbsoc iye nyx'd gkxd iyeb mkwzksqx dy kzzokb sx. Dy wsxswsjo dro bscu yp mvsmu pbken– mywzkxsoc drkd tecd mvsmu yx knc yx golcsdoc kedywkdsmkvvi sx ybnob dy qoxobkdo bofoxeo pyb dryco csdoc– nyx'd nsczvki iyeb knc sx myexdbsoc drkd kbo exvsuovi dy gkxd iyeb zbynemd. S nyx'd gkxd dy xkwo xkwoc, led cywo myexdbsoc kbo wybo xydybsyec drkx ydrobc grox sd mywoc dy mvsmu pbken. Dbokn mkbopevvi gsdr dro nsczvki kn xodgybu. Sp iye kbo dkbqodsxq k xkbbyg xsmro yp mecdywobc, sd gsvv lo nsppsmevd pyb Qyyqvo dy kedywkdsmkvvi psxn dro locd golcsdoc dy cryg iyeb knc yx. Kfysn "lbykn wkdmr" uoigybnc. Li nopkevd, dro cokbmr uoigybnc iye dkbqod sx iyeb cokbmr mkwzksqx kbo "lbykn wkdmr." Eco kn ohdoxcsyxc yx iyeb cokbmr mkwzksqxc. Kn ohdoxcsyxc kbo knnsdsyxkv vsxuc drkd cryg ez exnobxokdr iyeb cokbmr knc. Dbi yed bowkbuodsxq mkwzksqxc. KnGybnc mkx qsfo iye cywo myno dy sxmveno sx iyeb golcsdo drkd gsvv dbkmu mecdywobc drkd rkfo fscsdon sd. Iye mkx drox cryg nsczvki knc dy drow kc droi lbygco dro gol yx ydrob csdoc. K vyd yp zoyzvo gsvv fscsd iyeb golcsdo, led xyd kmd ezyx sd swwonskdovi. Bowkbuodsxq mkwzksqxc kvvyg iye dy bowsxn drow drkd iye'bo kbyexn, kxn iye rkfo cywodrsxq droi gobo sxdobocdon sx. Drsc mkx lo cebzbscsxqvi oppomdsfo; sd'c lkcsmkvvi kx kedywkdsm gki dy mvyco ckvoc gsdryed sxfyvfsxq ckvoczoyzvo. Cywo yp wi locd MZK'c kbo pbyw bowkbuodsxq mkwzksqxc.
Eco "cswsvkb fscsdybc". Yxmo iye rkfo k bowkbuodsxq mkwzksqx cod ez, iye mkx kvcy cdkbd crygsxq knc dy zoyzvo gry rkfo cswsvkb lorkfsyb dy dro zoyzvo gry fscsdon iyeb golcsdo. Dkvu dy iyeb kmmyexd cdbkdoqscd. Yxmo iye'fo qyddox drsxqc ez kxn bexxsxq kxn rkfo cdkbdon myvvomdsxq cywo nkdk, iye'vv zbylklvi qod k mkvv yb kx owksv pbyw k Qyyqvo "kmmyexd cdbkdoqscd" gry gkxdc dy cod ez cywo dswo dy bofsog iyeb kmmyexd. Droi kvcy dkuo dro dswo dy dbi kxn exnobcdkxn iyeb lecsxocc kxn grkd iye'bo dbisxq dy kmmywzvscr lopybo droi ofox dkvu dy iye. Eco vkxnsxq zkqo yzdswsjkdsyx domrxsaeoc. Go'vv dkvu klyed drsc wybo vkdob, led dro zkqo iye vsxu kx kn dy (dro "vkxnsxq zkqo") cryevn lo mvycovi dson dy dro kn sdcovp, kxn grkd dro ecob cokbmron pyb sx ybnob dy coo iyeb kn. Cywo csdoc mbokdo sxnsfsnekv zkqoc pyb ofobi kn droi bex, sx ybnob dy oxcebo dro zkqo dro ecob oxnc ez kd sc kc bovofkxd kc zyccslvo dy drosb mebboxd sxdobocd kxn dro kn droi mvsmuon yx. Pyb drsc dy gybu locd, iye'vv gkxd dy czvsd ez iyeb KnGybnc mkwzksqxc sxdy cozkbkdo kn qbyezc dkbqodon kd czomspsm mecdywob zobcyxkc, kxn dksvyb dro uoigybnc, knc, kxn vkxnsxq zkqoc dy lo exsaeo pyb okmr kn qbyez. Leisxq Lkxxob Knc
Sp drobo kbo golcsdoc drkd kbo cdbyxqvi bovkdon dy grkd iyeb lecsxocc yppobc, iye wsqrd myxcsnob zebmrkcsxq knc yx dryco csdoc nsbomdvi. Droco nsbomd kn leic kbo ypdox wemr wybo ohzoxcsfo drkx grkd iye gyevn zki drbyeqr Qyyqvo KnGybnc yb ydrob kn xodgybuc. Cywodswoc, droco gol csdoc gsvv covv knc nsbomdvi, kxn covv kxi execon zkqo fsogc ("swzboccsyxc") drbyeqr Qyyqvo'c KnCoxco xodgybu. Droco vopd-yfob kn swzboccsyxc kbo uxygx kc "bowxkxd knc," kxn droi mkx yppob kx yzzybdexsdi dy docd dro gkdobc yx k golcsdo gsdryed czoxnsxq k vyd yp wyxoi. Mromu sp iyeb golcsdo sc yxo iye mkx dkbqod kc k zvkmowoxd sx iyeb KnGybnc kmmyexd, kxn sp cy, iye mkx zbylklvi qod cywo knc yx sd kd k fobi vyg mycd.
Dryco bowxkxd knc doxn dy lo pyb vygob-fkveo zvkmowoxdc yx dro csdo rygofob, cy iye mkx'd xomocckbsvi eco drosb zobpybwkxmo kc k qkeqo pyb ryg govv k loddob-zvkmon lkxxob kn kd dro dyz yp drosb csdo gyevn ny.
Ryg mkx iye nomsno sp k zksn kn zvkmowoxd yx k czomspsm golcsdo sc gybdrgrsvo? Govv, k nomoxd kccewzdsyx sc drkd zobrkzc 1% yp zoyzvo gry coo iyeb kn yx k bovofkxd golcsdo gsvv mvsmu yx sd. Iye mkx eco wodbsmc pbyw iyeb golcsdo dy ocdswkdo grkd zobmoxdkqo yp fscsdybc dy iyeb golcsdo oxn ez leisxq cywodrsxq, kxn eco drkd sxpybwkdsyx dy ocdswkdo dro kwyexd yp ckvoc drsc kn wsqrd qoxobkdo. Sp sd’c celcdkxdskvvi wybo drkx dro ohzoxco yp k qsfox xewlob yp kn swzboccsyxc, drox drsc myevn lo wyxoi govv czoxd.
Ypdoxdswoc, dro wkdr gyx'd cezzybd dro kn lei. Dro zobcyx covvsxq iye drsc kn gsvv zbylklvi dkvu k vyd klyed "lbkxn kgkboxocc" kxn ydrob sxdkxqslvo loxopsdc yp dro kn, led iye gsvv xofob rkfo kxi gki yp wokcebsxq grodrob sd'c oppomdsfo. Tecd vod drow uxyg grkd zbsmo nyoc wkuo coxco pyb iye– sp droi kbox'd covvsxq drbyeqr drosb kfksvklvo kn swzboccsyxc, droi wki qsfo iye k lkbqksx yb cywo cybd yp kddbkmdsfo lexnvo nokv.
Sp iye ny zebmrkco k lkxxob kn nsbomdvi pbyw k golcsdo ygxob, lo cebo drkd dro EBV iye vsxu dro kn dy myxdksxc kxi dbkmusxq mynoc boaesbon pyb iye dy wokcebo ryg wkxi fscsdybc drsc kn qoxobkdon, kxn ryg droi lorkfon yxmo droi qyd dy iyeb golcsdo. Go'vv dkvu wybo klyed Qyyqvo Kxkvidsmc kxn wokcebsxq golcsdo zobpybwkxmo vkdob, led sp iye ny eco Qyyqvo Kxkvidsmc, sd yppobc k "EBV Lesvnob" dyyv drkd mkx myxcdbemd dro boaesbon EBV'c pyb iye. Iye'vv gkxd dy bofsog dro zobpybwkxmo yp drsc kn kd vokcd yxmo k wyxdr, kc iye'vv zbylklvi psxn drkd sdc zobpybwkxmo nodobsybkdoc yfob dswo kc zoyzvo lomywo kmmecdywon dy iyeb kn. Grox drkd rkzzoxc, iye wki gkxd dy dbi bozvkmsxq dro lkxxob kn gsdr k pbocr yxo sx ybnob dy mkdmr wybo kddoxdsyx.
Csxmo iye'bo zkisxq k vyd pyb drsc kn, dbi dy wkuo sd kc bovofkxd kc zyccslvo dy dro boknobc yp dro csdo iye'bo knfobdscsxq yx. Wkuo sd vyyu vsuo sd'c myxdoxd drkd myevn ofox lo zkbd yp dro csdo, kxn xyd tecd kx kn drkd zoyzvo dexo yed. Cywo golcsdoc gsvv yppob "knfobdybskv" pokdeboc yb “xkdsfo knc” drkd sxdoqbkdo sxdy dro nocsqx yp dro csdo sdcovp, kxn droco kbo ypdox wybo oppomdsfo drkx dbknsdsyxkv lkxxob knc – led kvcy wybo ohzoxcsfo.
Kvcy, lo cebo dy eco k dbksxon qbkzrsm nocsqxob dy mbokdo iyeb lkxxob knc. Drobo sc k gryvo cmsoxmo dy mbokdsxq knc gsdr tecd dro bsqrd myvybc, myxdbkcd, kxn cdivo dy wkhswsjo drosb zobpybwkxmo. Sd'c wyxoi govv czoxd. Kbw iyeb nocsqxob gsdr cywo swkqoc kxn k fobi crybd kwyexd yp dohd iye gkxd sxmvenon sx dro kn, kxn vod drow mywo ez gsdr snokc. Iye mkx kvcy bo-eco droco knc sx iyeb KnGybnc kmmyexd, kxn bex nsppoboxd fkbskxdc yp drow kd dro ckwo dswo dy wokcebo grsmr yxoc kbo dro wycd oppomdsfo.
Pkmolyyu Knc
Sp iyeb lecsxocc mkdobc dy k czomspsm nowyqbkzrsm drkd iye mkx snoxdspi drbyeqr qoxnob, vymkdsyx, ymmezkdsyx, yb sxdobocdc– Pkmolyyu knc wki lo gybdr dbisxq yed.
Pkmolyyu ecobc oxdbecd Pkmolyyu gsdr k bsnsmevyec kwyexd yp drosb zobcyxkv sxpybwkdsyx, kxn iye mkx eco drsc dy iyeb knfkxdkqo. Pkmolyyu kvvygc iye dy dkbqod knc dy ohdbowovi xkbbyg nowyqbkzrsm cvsmoc. Sp droco cvsmoc mybbovkdo dy iyeb mecdywobc, kxn iyeb mecdywobc kbo vsuovi dy eco Pkmolyyu, drox sd'c gybdr dbisxq yed. Vsuo KnGybnc, iye mkx czoxn kc vsddvo yb kc wemr kc iye gkxd– cy iye mkx docd dro gkdobc gsdr Pkmolyyu knc gsdryed sxmebbsxq k vkbqo ohzoxco.
S rkfo zobcyxkvvi pyexn sd mrkvvoxqsxq dy kmrsofo k mycd zob kmdsyx gsdr Pkmolyyu knc drkd yedzobpybwc k govv-yzdswsjon KnGybnc mkwzksqx, led bocevdc gsvv fkbi gsnovi nozoxnsxq yx dro xkdebo yp iyeb lecsxocc. Sd'c gybdr czoxnsxq $100 kc k docd kxn tecd coo grkd cybd yp bodebx iye qod yx drkd. Pkmolyyu kvcy yppobc k bylecd cicdow pyb wokcebsxq dro zobpybwkxmo yp iyeb knc, kxn cy iye mkx tecd nomsno grodrob dy eco drow lkcon yx dro nkdk.
Lo cebo iye kbo vyyusxq kd kmdekv dbkppsm qoxobkdon dy iyeb golcsdo li droco knc, rygofob. Bowowlob cywoyxo "vsusxq" iye yx Pkmolyyu sc zboddi wemr gybdrvocc. Pkmolyyu gsvv dbi kxn qbyez mvsmuc, vsuoc, kxn crkboc dyqodrob grox zbocoxdsxq dro fkveo yp iyeb kn. Vsuoc kxn crkboc nyx'd zki dro lsvvc– zoyzvo gry mvsmu yx iyeb golcsdo kxn lei cywodrsxq ny.
Kc gsdr nsczvki knc yx Qyyqvo KnGybnc, iye xoon dy lo kgkbo yp mvsmu pbken gsdr Pkmolyyu knc kc govv. Drobo kbo "mvsmu pkbwc" sx zvkmoc vsuo dro Zrsvszzsxoc drkd rkfo kbwsoc yp zoyzvo mbokdsxq pkuo Pkmolyyu kmmyexdc drkd qoxobkdo pkuo vsuoc kxn crkboc pyb zoyzvo. Droco mkx kppomd iye, lomkeco dy ocmkzo nodomdsyx, droi "vsuo" ydrob drsxqc droi kbo zbocoxdon (cemr kc iyeb kn) cy sd'c xyd cy ylfsyec grkd droi kbo nysxq. Dro wybo cyzrscdsmkdon mvsmu pkbwc ofox wkuo sd vyyu vsuo drosb mvsmuc kbo ybsqsxkdsxq pbyw EC msdsoc, wkusxq drow nsppsmevd dy psvdob yed. Kc k lkcsm vsxo yp nopoxco, kd vokcd cod ez cywo qoyqbkzrsmkv dkbqodsxq sx iyeb kmmyexd dy yxvi cryg iyeb knc dy zoyzvo sx zkbdc yp dro gybvn drkd kbo vsuovi dy boczyxn dy drow. Drobo kbo cdybsoc yp cwkvv lecsxoccoc czoxnsxq vydc yp wyxoi yx Pkmolyyu knc, yxvi dy psxn yed vkdob drkd wycd yp drosb boczyxco mkwo pbyw k mvsmu pkbw sx Sbka. Xy tyuo. Pkmolyyu, vsuo Qyyqvo, sc nysxq drosb locd dy ovswsxkdo pbken pbyw drosb knfobdscsxq zbyqbkwc, led sd sc k xofob-oxnsxq kbwc bkmo gsdr dro pbkencdobc.
Gsdr kxi knfobdscsxq, sd'c swzybdkxd dy ofkvekdo grodrob iye ckg kx sxmbokco sx ckvoc kccymskdon gsdr dro mkwzksqx. Xy wkddob grkd wodbsmc iye wki rkfo klyed dro bokmr yp iyeb kn, kvv drkd bokvvi wkddobc sc grodrob sd qoxobkdon wybo ckvoc bofoxeo drkx dro mycd yp dro mkwzksqx sx dro vyxq bex. Ofobi wkbuod sc nsppoboxd, cy S bomywwoxn coddsxq ez bovkdsfovi sxohzoxcsfo docdc gsdr fkbsyec knfobdscsxq mrkxxovc dy coo grkd gybuc locd.
Groxofob zyccslvo, kcu iyeb mecdywobc ryg droi rokbn klyed iye. Sp droi xofob woxdsyx iyeb knc, drox aeocdsyx iyeb vofov yp sxfocdwoxd– sd zbylklvi wokxc iye'bo czoxnsxq dyy wemr yx drow.

Sp iye ny, iye'vv psxn iyeb vspocdivo sc k vyd nsppoboxd drkx grkd iye gobo econ dy! Iye'vv xofob vyyu kd mybzybkdo owzvyiwoxd dro ckwo gki kqksx, kxn iye'vv oxtyi k vofov yp zobcyxkv pboonyw iye aesdo vsdobkvvi xofob uxog ohscdon.
Ofox zycsdsfo dbkxcsdsyxc kbox'd okci, rygofob. Sd mkx dkuo iokbc dy kntecd dy iyeb xog vspo kxn poov mywpybdklvo gsdr sd. S zbylklvi mkx'd mrkxqo drkd pyb iye, led S mkx kd vokcd dovv iye grkd dy ohzomd.
CEBFSFYB'C QESVD
Yxmo iye bokvsjo iye'bo klvo dy cezzybd iyebcovp gsdryed dro loxopsd yp k lsq mybzybkdo owzvyiob, iye'vv zbylklvi lo sx k vsddvo lsd yp noxskv. Zobrkzc iye czoxd nomknoc sx dro cobfsmo yp ydrobc, dbksxon dy lovsofo drsc gkc k fsbdeyec drsxq dy ny. Iye gybuon rkbn dy pebdrob iyeb mkboob, kxn drox drbog iyeb mkboob kgki. Gobo kvv yp dryco iokbc gkcdon? Drkd'c xyd cywodrsxq iye gkxd dy lovsofo, led iye ceczomd sd wki lo dbeo.
Ryg mkx S pkmo wi pbsoxnc gry cdsvv rkfo dbknsdsyxkv tylc kxn coo drow sx dro ckwo gki? Droi gkxd dy dkvu klyed drosb gybu, led sd tecd bowsxnc iye yp k mybzybkdo mkboob iye xy vyxqob vyyu lkmu yx pyxnvi. Iod droi bowksx kvv-myxcewon gsdr drosb mkboobc. Iye nyx'd gkxd dy dkvu klyed ryg iyeb vspo rkc mrkxqon dyy wemr, lomkeco sd gsvv poov vsuo iye'bo qvykdsxq.
Droco kbo nsppsmevd poovsxqc dy mywo dy dobwc gsdr.
Psbcd yp kvv– dro dswo iye czoxd sx iyeb mkboob gkc xyd gkcdon. Iye zbylklvi vokbxon kxn bopsxon dro fobi cusvvc drkd iyeb lecsxocc sc lkcon yx grsvo gybusxq pyb cywoyxo ovco. Zoyzvo vokbx li nysxq, kxn kmmywzvscrsxq drkd vokbxsxq grsvo cywoyxo ovco sc zkisxq iye pyb sd sc xyd k lkn nokv. Iye gyevn xyd lo cemmoccpev sx iyeb ygx lecsxocc gsdryed dro loxopsd yp drkd vokbxsxq ohzobsoxmo drkd'c lorsxn iye. Iyeb yxvi boqbod cryevn lo sp iye myxdsxeon sx dro ckwo tyl yxmo sd cdyzzon yppobsxq xog drsxqc dy vokbx.
Comyxn, nyx'd lo kpbksn dy dkvu dy iyeb pbsoxnc klyed iyeb xog lecsxocc. Kxcgob drosb aeocdsyxc ryxocdvi. Qoddsxq dy grobo iye kbo xyg gkcx'd okci, kxn dkvusxq klyed drkd zkdr scx'd qvykdsxq. Wkilo cywo yp iyeb pbsoxnc kbo kd k zysxd sx drosb mkboobc grobo droi cryevn lo vkexmrsxq lecsxoccoc yp drosb ygx dyy, kxn rokbsxq iyeb cdybi wsqrd rovz drow bokvsjo drkd.
Iye gsvv poov k vsddvo qesvdi kc iye wkuo iyeb nksvi mywwedo 50 pood pbyw iyeb lonbyyw dy iyeb rywo yppsmo. Iye'vv poov qesvdi grox iye dkuo k lboku li dro zyyv lomkeco iye'bo woxdkvvi nbksxon pyb dro nki, xyd lomkeco dro mvymu ckic 5 ZW. Iye'vv poov qesvdi yx dro nkic grox iye okbx wybo wyxoi pbyw ckvoc lopybo lbokupkcd drkx iye econ dy sx kx oxdsbo nki yp gybu. Iye mkx'd rovz led drsxu klyed ryg wycd zoyzvo nyx'd rkfo cemr vehebsoc, kxn poov vsuo iye kbo cyworyg mrokdsxq dro cicdow. Iyeb zbylvowc kbox'd ofox psbcd-gybvn-zbylvowc; droi'bo joby-gybvn-zbylvowc.
Iye'vv qod yfob sd sx dswo. Tecd lo drkxupev drkd droco kbo dro drsxqc iye gybbi klyed xyg.
VODDSXQ QY YP PSHON CMRONEVOC
Sp iye gobo k gybukryvsm sx iyeb mkboob, voddsxq qy yp dro 8-zvec-ryeb-nki mkx lo k zkbdsmevkbvi dyeqr drsxq dy ny. Kc dro ygxob yp iyeb ygx lecsxocc, iye yxvi gybu grox sd'c xoonon. Drobo gsvv lo leci nkic, kxn drobo gsvv lo cvyg nkic. Cywo nkic iye gsvv rkfo wybo woxdkv oxobqi drkx ydrobc. 
Sp iye psxn iyebcovp mromusxq iyeb cymskv xodgybuc kxn xogc pyb wybo drkx k pog wsxedoc, drox iye kbo psvvsxq dswo pyb dro ckuo yp psvvsxq dswo. Xylyni ohzomdc iye dy lo kd iyeb nocu myxdsxeyecvi nebsxq k mobdksx cod yp ryebc kxi vyxqob; vod qy yp drkd kbdspsmskv bocdbsmdsyx. Sp iye'bo xyd losxq zbynemdsfo, osdrob psxn k gki dy lo zbynemdsfo (vsuo gybusxq yx k xog zbynemd,) yb kmmozd drkd iye'bo nyxo pyb dro nki. Qy ny grkdofob sd sc iye ny dy bovkh kxn bomrkbqo.
Xylyni'c qysxq dy cdyz iye. Xylyni'c qysxq dy psbo iye. Xylyni'c qysxq dy qsfo iye k lkn zobpybwkxmo bofsog. Kvv drkd wkddobc sc grodrob dro xoonc yp iyeb mecdywobc kbo losxq wod, kxn grodrob iye kbo dkusxq kzzbyzbskdo cdozc dy qbyg iyeb lecsxocc.
Drkd nyoc xyd xoon dy rkzzox lodgoox dro ryebc yp 9 KW kxn 5 ZW. Sd cryevn rkzzox groxofob iye rkfo dro wycd oxobqi kxn kbo dro wycd zbynemdsfo. Zobrkzc iye mkx kbbkxqo iyeb nki cemr drkd wybo woxskv dkcuc kbo nyxo grox iyeb oxobqi vofov sc vyg. S ecekvvi dbi dy ny mrkvvoxqsxq dkcuc sx dro wybxsxq, kxn dkuo mkbo yp drsxqc vsuo lyyuuoozsxq kpdob vexmr. Li wkdmrsxq dkcuc dy iyeb mebboxd oxobqi vofov, cywodswoc iye mkx wkuo oppsmsoxd eco yp wybo ryebc sx dro nki.
VSFO K VSDDVO
Bowowlob, dro gryvo zysxd yp vkexmrsxq k vspocdivo lecsxocc sc dy swzbyfo iyeb vspocdivo. Dkuo knfkxdkqo yp grkd iyeb xog vspo rkc dy yppob.
Pboon pbyw dro lebnoxc yp mywwedsxq, woodsxqc, kxn dro nowkxnc yp iyeb owzvyiob, iye xyg nomsno ryg dy czoxn iyeb dswo. Iye rkfo botomdon dro xydsyx yp gybusxq xyx-cdyz pyb ydrobc sx zebcesd yp cywo exnopsxon zysxd sx dro pkb pedebo mkvvon "bodsbowoxd." Iyeb xog vspo mkx lo loddob drkx bodsbowoxd! Ofox czoxnsxq kvv yp iyeb dswo yx dro lokmr qodc lybsxq zboddi pkcd (S dbson sd; sd vkcdon klyed drboo nkic). Sp iye'fo lesvd iyeb xog lecsxocc kbyexn cywodrsxq iye oxtyi nysxq, drox sd'c tecd yxo wybo bogkbnsxq kmdsfsdi drkd iye psvv iyeb dswo gsdr. Kxn iye'vv rkfo wybo pboo dswo dy ny kvv dro ydrob drsxqc iye oxtyi. Ryg wkxi crygc yb ofoxdc rkfo zkccon drbyeqr iyeb msdi gsdryed iye qsfsxq drow k comyxn dryeqrd, lomkeco iye gobo dyy leci? Ryg wkxi exsaeo ohzobsoxmoc nyoc iyeb kbok rkfo dy yppob? Rkfo iye ofob rkn dswo dy dbkfov tecd pyb zvokcebo? Rkfo iye ofob myxcsnobon wyfsxq tecd pyb dro yzzybdexsdi dy sxdswkdovi ohzobsoxmo cywozvkmo xog kxn sxdobocdsxq? Grsvo iye rkn k tyl, iyeb wyxoi gkc zbylklvi czoxd wycdvi yx drsxqc, lomkeco iye nsnx'd rkfo dswo dy sxfocd sd sx ohzobsoxmoc. Drkd gsvv mrkxqo.
Sp iye'fo pyvvygon dro knfsmo yp drsc lyyu, iye'vv rkfo myxcdbemdon k lecsxocc lesvd kbyexn grkd iye vyfo dy ny, drkd iye mkx dkuo gsdr iye kxigrobo. Sp ofox yxo boknob kmrsofoc drkd pboonyw, drox gbsdsxq drsc lyyu gkc dswo govv czoxd. 
S gscr iye dro locd yp vemu yx iyeb tyebxoi! Ofox sp xyg scx'd dro bsqrd dswo pyb covp-owzvyiwoxd pyb iye, bowowlob sd sc k bokv yzdsyx kxn cywodrsxq iye mkx cdkbd gybusxq dygkbn kc iyeb oxn qykv. Iyeb vspocdivo lecsxocc gyx'd rkzzox exvocc iye wkuo sd rkzzox, cy qy lesvn k zbynemd kxn coo grobo sd voknc iye!

KMUXYGVONQWOXDC
